Tensions in the French Chamber of Deputies; Laval Engages in Heated Debate; Socialist Leader Faints During Speech; Government Likely to Win Confidence Vote 41

Paris – Premier Laval engaged in a heated debate in the Chamber of Deputies this morning, defending his political life. Deputies from various parties held differing views on Laval's foreign policy. However, Laval remained calm. After a period of debate, the Chamber adjourned until 3:00 PM this afternoon, at which time Laval will deliver his final defense speech. At 6:00 PM, the Chamber will vote on the confidence issue concerning his foreign policy. Well-informed sources believe that everything hinges on Laval's ability to convince a small number of undecided deputies to salvage the situation. (National Telegram, 28th)

Paris – The atmosphere in the Chamber of Deputies was quite tense during Premier Laval's speech today. Socialist leader Blum then spoke, strongly criticizing Laval. Right-wing deputies interrupted him, infuriating the socialist deputies, who stood up and swung punches at those interrupting. The session was temporarily suspended. After a brief rest, Blum resumed his speech, stating that if all nations firmly supported the League of Nations, there would be no danger of war. Laval, however, was deliberately creating an atmosphere of impending war, and therefore should be asked to resign. Left-wing deputies applauded enthusiastically. Central party deputy Reynaud praised England and criticized Laval's policy, saying that Italy was an aggressor nation, while England was a supporter of the League of Nations covenant. France must choose between the two. About two-thirds of the deputies, from the extreme left to the central right, cheered upon hearing this warning. Observers called this the death knell for the current government. Others predicted that even if the Laval government won, it would only be by a margin of 20 to 30 votes. (Reuters, 28th)

Paris – The Chamber of Deputies reconvened at 9:00 AM this morning for the foreign policy debate, with only ten deputies and one cabinet member in attendance. Premier Laval arrived quite early, looking very tired, having stayed up all night preparing his speech. Judging by appearances, the government's position is very precarious. However, many radicals are still hesitant, unwilling to overthrow the Laval government before the budget is passed, thus potentially triggering a serious political crisis. Laval's biggest political opponent, Mr. Caillaux, has decided not to attack Laval today. Meanwhile, the opposition has introduced a motion stating that the government has failed to create a clear impression that the world trusts the policies France has followed since 1919, which is regrettable. It also stated that the inseparability of national security and the League of Nations covenant should be the primary consideration. Central party deputy Champetier de Ribes introduced a vote of confidence in the government, stating that the government must respect the covenant while seeking peace. All speakers at this morning's meeting were brief, after which the session adjourned until 3:00 PM this afternoon. (Reuters, 28th)

Paris – The Chamber of Deputies continued discussing the government's foreign policy this morning for three hours, until 12:05 PM, when it adjourned. Deputies delivered brief speeches, either defending or opposing the government. Radical Socialist Party leader Herriot also presented a motion stating that since 1919, the foundation of French foreign policy has been respect for the League of Nations covenant and national security. The government's attitude toward the Italo-Ethiopian dispute has failed to create this impression on the world, which is regrettable. The Chamber is scheduled to reconvene at 3:10 PM this afternoon and is expected to vote around 4:00 PM. (Havas, 28th)

Paris – Seventy-three deputies are expected to speak on current affairs. The confidence vote on Laval's policy will be held at 4:00 PM on Saturday afternoon. Socialist leader Blum continued to criticize Laval, accusing him of failing to notify Italian Prime Minister Mussolini earlier of France's opposition to Italy's ambition to conquer Ethiopia. He called Laval the culprit for weakening the forces of peace. Blum fainted at this point due to over-excitement, but quickly regained consciousness and continued his speech. The Radical Socialist Party will be split over the confidence issue, which may give Laval an additional 30 to 40 votes. (National Telegram, 27th)

Paris – In the Chamber of Deputies' lounge, it is generally predicted that the government will win the afternoon vote by a majority of about twenty votes. Premier and Foreign Minister Laval plans to offer a response after the final questions are asked, between 3:30 PM and 3:45 PM, and immediately demand a vote. (Havas, 28th)

Paris – The extreme left, central party, and Republican Party have decided to support the government, so Laval's chances of victory in the Chamber of Deputies today have improved. The stock exchange expects the government to win by a majority of twenty votes. (Reuters, 28th)

Laval's Speech; Vigorously Defending Foreign Policy; Unwavering Commitment to Mediating Peace; No Regret Over Abandoned Plan 42

Paris – At 3:00 PM today, Premier and Foreign Minister Laval attended the Chamber of Deputies and delivered an important speech regarding the international situation since the resignation of former British Foreign Secretary Hoare and the failure of the plan proposed by England and France. He stated: "The Italian government did not study the plan proposed by England and France with enthusiasm and understanding, which was contrary to our expectations. Furthermore, Prime Minister Mussolini's speech in the new village of Pontinia did not facilitate our efforts to mediate the dispute. Although our efforts have been thwarted, I do not regret it, because peace will eventually be restored. Today's debate in the Chamber of Deputies, I believe, has three main questions: 1. Does the policy I have pursued conform to the interests of France? 2. Have I abandoned France's commitment to the League of Nations? 3. Has the security of France, both present and future, been harmed by me?" We should seek clarity on these three points. Laval then explained that France had accepted the sanctions and was strictly implementing them, stating, "I have declared to England that if it is attacked by Italy for implementing sanctions, France will provide assistance by sea, land, and air. I do not hesitate to offer this guarantee from France, knowing that I have assumed a great responsibility, which is unavoidable as a result of the League of Nations covenant. My duty is to ease relations between England and Italy in every way possible, because I believe that the more stringent our obligations under the League of Nations covenant, the more we should seek a peaceful resolution in every way possible." Laval then cited a statement by former British Foreign Secretary Hoare in the House of Commons, saying that Italy considers the oil embargo to be a military sanction, which is tantamount to war against Italy. Laval then praised Hoare as a man and said, "The plan proposed by England and France has indeed been abandoned, but the path to reconciliation remains open. The sanctions adopted by various countries in the economic and financial fields are already very severe. Who dares say that they are ineffective? If we expand the scope of sanctions, who dares guarantee that the scope of the conflict will not expand?" Laval then responded to some who accused him of abandoning international law, saying, "The purpose of international law is to prevent the outbreak of war in advance and to limit its impact afterward, not to expand the war and make it spread. The purpose of sanctions is to restore peace, but sanctions themselves are not an end, but only a means to an end. If the goal can be achieved more easily through negotiations, then negotiations are not only permitted by the League of Nations covenant, but also our duty, which the League of Nations should always remember." Laval then responded to some who accused the French government's attitude toward the Italo-Ethiopian dispute of reducing the chances of other countries helping France if it were attacked, saying that cooperation between England and France has always been the cornerstone of European security. "The unity of England and France has not been harmed because of me alone. I have no complaints that England ultimately rejected the plan that had already been drafted. In short, I do not regret what I have done in the past, and in the future, no matter what, I will continue to work tirelessly for peace." (Havas, 17th)

Leaders of Left-Wing Parties; Eloquent and Passionate Speeches; Refuting Laval's Misleading the Country 43

Paris – At 3:00 PM today, the Chamber of Deputies discussed the government's foreign policy. Premier and Foreign Minister Laval first delivered a lengthy speech, explaining the international situation after the resignation of former British Foreign Secretary Hoare and defending the government's current foreign policy. Orthodox leader Léon Blum then spoke, refuting Laval's policy with passionate words, saying that its aim was to please Italy and show disloyalty to the League of Nations covenant. As a result, France's allies, including the small countries of Central Europe, have been disheartened. He concluded that the best way to ensure France's security was to obtain the full assistance of England and Russia. Next, Mr. Taittinger, leader of the right-wing "Patriotic Youth League," spoke, saying that during the European War, England and Italy cooperated with France, the value of which is worth remembering. Therefore, the current cabinet should remain strictly neutral on the Italo-Ethiopian issue, without taking sides. If military sanctions are to be taken against Italy in the future, a mobilization order should be submitted to the Chamber of Deputies for approval, then he and his comrades will not bear the responsibility for the vote. After Taittinger finished speaking, Radical Socialist Party leader Herriot spoke, saying that Laval's policy, while claiming to uphold the League of Nations covenant, was too weak and, on the other hand, was enough to encourage and reward Italy's determination to resist sanctions and Germany's attempt to take advantage of the situation. Herriot concluded by saying that because the government adopted this policy, the Radical Socialist Party caucus could not express confidence in the current cabinet. After he finished speaking, most of the Radical Socialist Party deputies applauded and cheered in unison. Judging from the attitude of the Radical Socialist Party deputies, the trend of the party's vote on the confidence issue can be roughly seen. At this point, Mr. Renault, chairman of the Central Republican Party caucus and former Minister of Finance, spoke, saying that Germany's main goal was to alienate the relationship between England and France. It is paying close attention to the development of the current international crisis. Therefore, it is not in France's interest to allow the bonds between England and France to loosen. As for the League of Nations covenant, even if Franco-Italian friendship is deep, it should still be faithfully fulfilled and should not be wavering. By this time it was 10:00 PM, and the Chamber of Deputies adjourned and continued the discussion tomorrow morning. The government's vote of confidence is scheduled to be held tomorrow afternoon. Looking at the speeches of the deputies today, the most outstanding was Renault's. Although Renault belongs to the central faction, even opposition deputies cheered during his eloquent speech. What he said may affect the outcome of the vote of confidence tomorrow afternoon. Laval hopes to gain a majority of about twenty-five votes at that time. (Havas, 27th)

Paris – In the Chamber of Deputies' debate on foreign policy this afternoon, the speech by Mr. Renault, chairman of the Central Republican Party caucus and former Minister of Finance, was the most outstanding. It won applause from the central and extreme left-wing deputies. The main points have been covered in previous telegrams, and the main points of the speech are supplemented below:

Renault said, "Since the Great War, we have repeatedly questioned England about the issue of automatically enacting sanctions under the League of Nations covenant. Only now have the English people answered directly, yes. This is a good opportunity, but we have failed to understand it." Renault then gave examples to explain the errors in the French public opinion's judgment of England's attitude. He also said that even if Abyssinia is conquered by the Italian army, Italy's population problem cannot be solved. "For example, in Italian Eritrea, there are currently 400,000 natives, but only 4,000 European expatriates. Even if 100,000 Italians can live and reproduce in Abyssinia in the future, Italy's population problem will still not be solved." If Italy had previously adopted a peaceful invasion method toward Abyssinia, the League of Nations would not have blocked Italy's path. "We cherish the Italian people deeply, and therefore we regret their misguided path greatly." Renault continued that since the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has rejected peaceful proposals four times. The reason for this is not for material interests, but because the principles on which the League of Nations is based conflict with Fascism. Fascism has clearly declared that men dying on the battlefield is a matter of course, just like women should devote themselves to motherhood. Renault concluded by saying that France has the great British Empire on one hand and Italy, which is going against the League of Nations, on the other. Which should we follow? Will we bury the great hopes that arose after the European War, or will we bet on this move? (Havas, 27th)

Science vs. Nature 46

Bombers Change Direction of Volcanic Lava

Hilo – Modern science is battling nature today. A squadron of American bombers has dropped bombs on Mauna Loa volcano in an attempt to change the direction of the lava flow. One aircraft dropped six 100-pound bombs on the lava flowing down the mountainside. Other aircraft flew to the top of the volcano and dropped bombs into the crater, aiming to block its exit and divert the lava to another direction. Whether this experiment will be effective is still unknown. The volcano had been dormant for two years and erupted again last month. Its lava has now flowed to within four miles of Hilo's water reservoir. (Reuters, 27th)

Two concubines have left, and one is living with a friend in Jinan. Due to the severe cold, he begged to be allowed to temporarily shelter in the warming station. The station, finding his story pitiable, allowed him to enter. (Special dispatch, 28th)

At the same time, twenty groups issued another telegram, stating that after the Zhangzhou rice tax was levied, exports this month were only 1,700 to 1,800 bags, whereas in the same month last year, during peak season, there were that many bags per day. Song Zheyuan's Mission to Tianjin 91

Exchanging Opinions with Doihara

The Hebei-Chahar Political Council Postpones One Meeting, Beiping Communication: Since the establishment of the government committee, the Hebei-Chahar situation and the administrative organization have been completely renewed, and internal problems have been almost nonexistent. However, after the establishment of the council, the most pressing task is not personnel arrangements, but how to deal with foreign affairs, in order to strengthen the people's belief in the responsible authorities of the council. During the gestation period of the new political system in Hebei-Chahar, Xiao Zhenying, who was responsible for foreign affairs, declared to the press on November 18 that if the new political system is realized, the Tanggu Agreement can be abolished and the administrative powers of Hebei Province will be completely restored. The Japanese side had promised to return Dolun, which had been occupied. Song Zheyuan, the Commander of the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison, who was stationed in Beiping, also stated that he would definitely achieve the above two points. These were all clearly stated. However, in reality, as of now, Dolun has not been recovered. Bordering the area, Guyuan, Changbao, Kangbao, Shangdu, Huade, and Zhangbei six counties, the Japanese side, under the pretext of wanting to complete its Manchu-Mongolian policy, actually had the puppet army of Li Shouxin invade under the cover of airplanes and artillery. As of now, the situation in these six counties is unknown because the intelligence from Zhangjiakou has not mentioned it, which is deeply concerning to the people of the country. Given that the situation is such, the issue of recovering Dolun is indeed one of the urgent concerns of the authorities. Secondly, there is the "Eastern Hebei" issue. Since its establishment on November 25, the puppet organization of Eastern Hebei has been in existence for exactly one month as of this month's 25th. Under the direction of the Japanese, Yin Rugeng issued another declaration, renaming it the "Autonomous Government." This move is ominous and seems to be a challenge to the Hebei-Chahar authorities. On the very day of the council's establishment, Chairman Song Zheyuan sent Xiao Zhenying and Qin Dechun to visit Doihara Kenji to propose negotiations for the cancellation of the "Eastern Hebei" puppet organization. Unexpectedly, the Japanese side went a step further, elevating the puppet organization by one step, declaring a name change, and expanding its area.

On the very day when the above news came out, Song Zheyuan, the Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, because his Chief of Staff Chen Juesheng was temporarily acting as the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, went to Tianjin with Chen at 3:05 pm on the 25th. Many people accompanied him. Until now, Song and his cadres are all in Tianjin, and Beiping is unusually empty. The Hebei-Chahar Political Council's regular meeting on the 27th was announced to be postponed once because most of the committee members were not in Beiping. Song's confidant Lei Sishang was also summoned to Tianjin on the evening of the 27th to participate in confidential matters. According to political circles, Song Zheyuan and others will stay in Tianjin for three or four days before returning. There is indeed contact with the Japanese side in Tianjin, but it can only be said that they are exchanging opinions, and there is still a considerable distance from formal negotiations. Judging from the contact in the past two days, it is of course considered necessary to discuss the expansion of the "Eastern Hebei" puppet organization first. As a result, after a hasty conversation with Doihara on the evening of the 25th in Tianjin, Doihara flew to Shenyang the next morning and then went to Changchun. After Doihara left Tianjin, there was a certain rumor here that the authorities of a certain city also flew there by Japanese plane, but it has yet to be confirmed. General observations suggest that there is considerable possibility. At the same time, there is also widespread speculation that the key to resolving the "Eastern Hebei" issue has been moved from Tianjin to Changchun. The reason is that Doihara's trip to the east this time, in addition to reporting on his stay in Beiping, will definitely request instructions on the issues of "Eastern Hebei," "Northern Chahar," and "Tanggu." It is expected that the leaders of the Kwantung Army will have an important agreement on the 27th and 28th, which will be brought back by Doihara for implementation. Therefore, it is understood that it will be difficult for our side to deal with these three matters. However, if the Hebei-Chahar Political Council cannot properly handle the current diplomacy, the internal and external impact will be incalculable. We are here only hoping that Song and Xiao will not break their previous words and will show great faith. (27th)

Japanese Troops Gradually Withdraw from Beiping and Tianjin 92

Garrison Troops in Yu, Qin, Return to Original Defense

Abandoned Aircraft Field in Juzi, East of Tianjin

Tianjin Communication: The issue of the Japanese military forcibly occupying land in Juzi, east of Tianjin, to build an airfield has been handed over to the Tianjin Office of the Provincial Government for negotiations after the changes in the political situation in Hebei Province, hoping to resolve it locally. As the office is being closed down, the negotiations have stalled. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Government to instruct the Tianjin-Dagu Security Command and the Tianjin County Government to carefully monitor the construction situation. Currently, the Tianjin-Dagu Security Command has also been suspended, and all monitoring responsibilities have been transferred to the Tianjin County Government. According to the county government's report to the province after investigation, the more than 100 Japanese Kwantung Army Air Force personnel stationed in the International Racecourse in Dongjuzi left Tianjin on the 20th and returned to outside the pass. On the 22nd, personnel from the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Headquarters went to the airfield to remove the aircraft landing markers and the Japanese flag, and the electrical wires and military telephones stored in the racecourse's large dining hall were also taken away. From the 19th to the 24th, all Japanese planes flying in from outside the pass landed at the Bali Tai Airfield in Nankai, Tianjin, and the Dongjuzi airfield was not used. When the situation in North China was urgent, the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Headquarters had announced that six air squadrons, a total of 60 aircraft, would come to Tianjin to participate in a large-scale joint air and land military exercise between Beiping, Tianjin, and Tanggu. Now that this matter has passed and there is no need for further exercises given the current situation, the large air squadrons have ceased to fly in. However, the Japanese military headquarters has not yet indicated whether it will use the airfield for its own convenience or return it after two months. According to the county government's investigation, the airfield occupies 13.4 hectares of land, with 5 hectares owned by the Beining Railway Bureau, 8 hectares owned by Li Chun (former Military Governor of Jiangsu), and 40 acres owned by six farmers, including Wang Deming. The total area of the airfield is approximately 1,500 square meters, 1,200 meters wide from east to west, with 880 meters leveled, and 760 meters long from north to south, with 130 meters leveled. Half of the occupied land is cultivated farmland. Although the Tianjin Japanese military had previously stated that it would pay rent per acre, our side considered it a forced occupation because the negotiations were not concluded and did not accept their proposal.

As for all the Japanese garrison troops in North China, which were deployed from Yu, Qin, Tang, Luan, Chang, and Tang areas to the cities of Beiping and Tianjin during the previous tense situation, and the Matsui and Suzuki brigades of the Kwantung Army, which were gathering from Jinzhou and Suiyuan areas to Shanhaiguan, are now returning to their original garrisons outside the pass from the 20th onward, given the stabilization of the situation and the lack of need to station heavy troops. A portion of the troops is being transferred to eastern Chahar, stationed in Fengning, awaiting orders in the direction of Chahar. The Japanese garrison troops originally stationed in Yu, Qin, Luan, and Tang areas have been returning to their original garrisons from Beiping and Tianjin in two batches since the 21st. Regarding the replenishment of the Japanese garrison troops in North China, there is no confirmed news on how many new troops will be added and when they will arrive, as the budget has not yet been approved. (25th)

Beiping Student Union Association慰问伤员同学 94

Holds Exhibition of Blood-Stained Clothing

Northeastern Middle School Students All on Hunger Strike

Beiping Communication: The student movement in Beiping has recently eased, but it has not become passive. On the 27th, the Student Union held a grand consolation meeting at the Yixian Hall of China University, firstly to console the students who were arrested and injured in the two petitions, and secondly to thank Chinese and foreign journalists and teachers and staff of various schools. The conference opened at 1:00 PM, with more than 1,000 male and female student representatives from more than 50 schools participating. The presidium consisted of three members, organized by Yanjing University, China University, and Peking University. There were more than 30 Chinese and foreign journalists. The students' attitude, amidst enthusiasm, contained a feeling of sadness. The details are as follows:

Strict Security

On both sides of the gate of China University, there were picket teams organized by male and female students, holding wooden sticks used by Boy Scouts and rifles prepared for military training. All guests and students entering the school had to present their admission tickets or business cards, or they would be refused entry. After being permitted by the picket team, another traffic team led them to the entrance of the Yixian Hall. At the second door of the Yixian Hall, there was a registration desk. After completing the registration procedure, after a few more steps, you were inside the Yixian Hall. At the hall door, there were patrol teams responsible for collecting admission tickets and guiding seating arrangements. The arrangement of the venue was very thorough.

Display of Blood-Stained Clothing

The Yixian Hall faces south from the north, so the podium was built on the west side, with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the Party and national flags hanging high. The opening ceremony was simple and hung at the top of the blackboard. The press box and the presidium were on the right side, and the injured students' rest area was on the left, with three soft beds, covered with luxurious Western pillows and bed sheets. Looking to the east, there was a yellow paper slogan hanging horizontally on the wall, "Blood-Soaked Ironclad Facts," below were thirteen pieces of blood-stained clothing of the injured students. On the right end were photos of the two petitions, totaling more than fifty photos, combined into five large panels. On the front table, there were more than one hundred consolation items, such as pastries, canned goods, fresh flowers, and fresh fruits. There were also more than a dozen commemorative mirrors made by the Student Union and presented to various schools, with the words "The Blood of Warriors, The Glory of Revolution" written on them. There were two larger mirrors, one inscribed with "Struggle" and the other with "Sacrifice," made and presented by the female students of No. 1 Girls' Middle School. The Jinghu Middle School also presented a banner inscribed with the four characters "National Fighters." At a glance, it was colorful and dazzling. The rest of the room was surrounded by slogans and colorful flowers.

China University's Consolation

In addition to participating in the consolation meeting as members, the students of China University, out of the courtesy of the host, organized a China University consolation team, specially made delicate flowers with pink silk ribbons. All injured students who entered the venue were personally decorated by the female consolation team members to express condolences and encouragement.

Participating Schools

The schools participating in the consolation meeting included Northeastern University, Fu Jen Catholic University, Normal University, Tsinghua University, Yenching University, Jiaotong University, Peking University, Beiping University (College of Law and Commerce, College of Agriculture, College of Engineering, Medical College, College of Liberal Arts for Women), Sino-French University, China College, Republic College, Chaoyang University, Jinghu Middle School, Liangji Girls' Middle School, Huiyi Middle School, Kongde Middle School, Dazhong Middle School, Northeast University Preparatory Class, Yiwu Middle School, Qiushi Middle School, Fu Jen Catholic University Affiliated Girls' Middle School, Jingshi Middle School, Huiwen Middle School, No. 53 Middle School, No. 1 Girls' Middle School, No. 2 Girls' Middle School, Jinde Middle School, Kongde Middle School, North China Middle School, Art College, Zhongshan Middle School, Chengcheng Middle School, Jingye Middle School, Duzhi Middle School, Yijiao Middle School, Datong Middle School, Mongolian and Tibetan School, Zhicheng Middle School, Hongda Middle School, and more than fifty schools.

Conference Situation

After the announcement of the opening of the meeting, everyone stood at attention and bowed to the arrested and injured students (three minutes of silence). Then, the chairman, a representative from Yenching University, reported on the significance of the consolation meeting in two points: 1. To take the opportunity of consoling the arrested and injured students to gather students from all over the city in one hall, report on past facts and experiences, review past mistakes, and plan future work. 2. To reward the press who provided public opinion assistance and the teachers and staff of various schools who gave well-intentioned advice during the student movement. At the same time, it is hoped that all guests will gain a deep understanding and guidance on the past and future of the student movement in Beiping at this grand consolation meeting.

Student Union Report

Then, the Student Union representative (Peking University student) reported on the work of the Student Union, stating, "The Beiping Student Union was born in response to the environment of the times. Since its organization, it has been very secretive due to environmental factors, so it is unknown to the outside world. Now, I will briefly report to you on the general situation. This union was established on November 18, when only Yiwu Middle School and Municipal No. 1 Girls' Middle School and other schools initiated it. Eight schools participated, with three representatives from each school. The first representative conference was held on the 18th. Then, after active preparations, the second representative conference was held at the end of November, with 17 schools participating, and it was decided to hold a petition on December 9. On the evening of the 8th, the third representative conference was held to prepare for the parade on the 9th. The fourth representative conference was held on the 18th, with 52 schools participating. The meeting lasted the longest, from 3:00 PM on the 18th to 8:00 AM the next morning. All motions were divided into four parts: 1. Determining future directions. 2. Formulating a work program. 3. Centralizing command power. 4. Consoling injured and arrested students."

Guest Speeches

After the speeches by Liu Yaohan, the representative of the arrested students, and Tong Zhizhong, the representative of the injured students, the Tianjin Student Union representative reported on the recent situation of the Tianjin Student Union's work to save the country, stating that 22 schools participated in the Tianjin student movement, with more than 7,000 students. The parade and petition on December 18 were not obstructed by the military police. The purpose of this trip to Beiping is to not only express condolences but also to connect with the Beiping Student Union and take consistent actions. Then, Yang Wenkui, the representative of the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff of National Colleges and Universities in Beiping and Tianjin, gave a speech expressing three points: 1. The student patriotic movement must have a perfect organization. 2. It is hoped that the spirit will be maintained forever. 3. The attitude must be calm. Then, students from various schools gave free speeches, shouted slogans, and the meeting adjourned at around 5:00 PM.

National Northeastern Zhongshan Middle School: All two hundred students have been on a hunger strike since the 27th. Representatives from various schools went to try to persuade them to eat, but the students of Zhongshan Middle School, because the Northeast has already fallen, reside in Beiping, and are often in danger of the Hebei problem, have no intention of eating. They wish to dedicate themselves to the country and recover the lost territory. Representatives from various schools are scheduled to make a second attempt to persuade them to eat on the 28th. According to people familiar with the situation of Northeastern Zhongshan Middle School, there are two reasons for the students' hunger strike: 1. The student movement in Beiping has recently declined. In order to encourage the patriotic sentiments of students, they are on a hunger strike to urge students from various schools to actively work to save the country. 2. The school's food expenses have long been allocated to the student union as office expenses. Now they only want to work and not eat, indicating that patriotism is more important than eating. (27th)

Wuhan Martial Law Measures 95

Divided into three zones, each with a martial law commander.

Traffic to be cut off from 12:00 PM nightly.

Assemblies and societies prohibited, and control over vehicles and vessels.

Hankou Communications, Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, following orders to impose martial law, began implementation on the evening of the 26th. However, due to late receipt of the Military Affairs Commission's telegram, public announcement was only made known on the morning of the 27th. Wuhan garrison is originally divided into three districts: Wuchang, Hankou, and Hanyang. Each district has a commander. This martial law decision will still follow the original area division. Martial Law Commander Chen Jicheng is ordered to appoint the three district garrison commanders, such as Shen Tingzhen, to concurrently serve as martial law commanders for each district, each responsible for their respective areas. The original text of the announcement reads: "Based on the Military Affairs Commission's telegram Youzi, and the National Government's order, and the reports from Songhu Garrison Commander, Nanjing Garrison Commander, Wuhan Garrison Commander, etc., since the North Peace student petition incident, evildoers have taken the opportunity to stir up trouble, attempting to incite rebellion, leading to public unrest and concerns about public safety. It is urgently necessary to order the Military Affairs Commission to declare martial law in necessary areas to maintain order. Acknowledge and take note, etc. Based on this, considering the importance of the Wuhan area, it should be declared under martial law immediately, and the commander appointed as the Wuhan area martial law commander. Faithfully and earnestly implement the law to ensure public safety. This order, etc. This headquarters, starting from today, will implement martial law in the garrison area according to martial law regulations. During this martial law period, traffic will be cut off every night from 12:00 PM until dawn the next day. Public officials must answer passwords and present passes to be allowed through. All others are prohibited from passing to prevent wrongdoing and ensure tranquility. In addition to separate orders and reports, this announcement is made to inform the public." Matters concerning the implementation of martial law areas: All assemblies and societies are to be suspended, and the publication of newspapers, magazines, pictures, advertisements, slogans, etc., deemed detrimental to public safety will be prohibited. Postal items and telegrams that are detrimental to public safety may be detained or confiscated. Vessels, vehicles, and aircraft entering or leaving the country must be subject to inspection by this headquarters. If necessary, traffic may be stopped, and major roads and routes may be blocked. Travelers deemed suspicious may be inspected. If necessary, private firearms, ammunition, weapons, fire tools, and other dangerous items may be inspected and detained or confiscated. During the martial law period, pedestrian traffic will be cut off every night from 12:00 PM until dawn the next day. Public officials traveling on official business must have a pass from this headquarters and answer passwords to be allowed through. Based on the situation, pedestrian checks and household registration spot checks may be implemented. During the martial law period, transportation vehicles and vessels within the garrison area will be controlled by the police department. A meeting of various transportation organizations is scheduled for the 28th to discuss appropriate measures to adapt to the environment without hindering traffic. (27th)

Qingdao Academic Community's Appeal for National Salvation 97

—Separate telegrams to the Ministry of Education and Song Zheyuan—

Qingdao Correspondence, Recently, students in Peiping and Tianjin have been conducting strikes out of deep patriotism as a national salvation movement, and students across the country have responded enthusiastically. The students of National Shandong University in Qingdao have also held meetings several times to discuss the establishment of a student national salvation committee as support for the students in Peiping and Tianjin. Mayor Shen Honglie, fearing that students did not understand the true facts and would cause misunderstandings, has summoned students from various secondary schools and above for talks to explain the true situation of the current situation and ordered them to focus on their studies and not to jeopardize their lives due to momentary impulsiveness. Therefore, students in other places are extremely active, but Qingdao is silent and unknown. However, teachers and students of Qingdao's large, medium, and small schools have also sent telegrams to the Ministry of Education and Song Zheyuan, which are copied as follows:

Telegram to the Ministry of Education

"Nanjing Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education, and forwarded to President Jiang of the Executive Yuan, Junjian, Recently, there has been a brewing of autonomy and separation in Peiping and Tianjin, and students there, with deep patriotism, have petitioned together. Officials have failed to investigate and have indiscriminately arrested and attacked them. The academic community in Qingdao shares deep sorrow and indignation. Recently, our local officials have repeatedly stated to teachers and students throughout the city the central government's determination to stabilize North China and maintain territorial sovereignty, and have urged them to strictly abide by the orders of the Executive Yuan and the Ministry to study diligently. Although faculty and staff will carefully follow the teachings and adhere to the scope, we are still unable to restrain ourselves from speaking out. It is said that the establishment of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council is a disguised form of the autonomous committee, which people get the substance of, and we take the name of it, which implies great worries for the future of North China. Judging by the past changes, it seems difficult to fully decide on our own. This is the first reason for public concern. It is also said that our country's diplomacy will take the facts as the premise, and the entire negotiation of the country as one thing, and the accomplished fact of North China as another thing, to deal with it in separate ways and endure and seek survival. If what is said is true, it is tantamount to withdrawing the fence ourselves. This is the second reason for public concern. Beiping is the cultural center of our country and the place where the national spirit lies. Now, when a great disaster is happening, there is no freedom to appeal. If the evolution becomes more intense in the future, what room will there be to study national affairs? The tragedy of the fox facing death and the rabbit crying is the same feeling for everyone. What will the country have without the national soul? This is the third reason for public concern. We think that the major plan of the country has already been calculated in the temple. Although we know that observing through a tube and measuring with a gourd cannot help the profound, we only use the meaning of everyone's responsibility to do our best to offer the wild man's sincerity. Urgent statement, not at all in fear and trembling, to await orders.

Qingdao Organizes Inspection Group to Beijing and Shanghai 98

—Inspects safety and sanitation conditions—

Qingdao Correspondence, The Qingdao Industrial Safety and Sanitation Committee held a temporary meeting at the Social Affairs Bureau at 3:00 PM on the 26th, chaired by Dong Zhidao, the second section chief of the Social Affairs Bureau. They discussed the measures for organizing a safety and sanitation inspection group to Beijing and Shanghai, proposed by three committee members: Yi Tianjue, Wang Shouze, and Chen Keyao. The measures were approved after discussion and submitted to the municipal government for approval. Once approved, they will head south after the Lunar New Year. The purpose of the inspection group is as follows: The Ministry of Industry is preparing a national industrial safety and sanitation exhibition, scheduled to be held in January next year, and has collected many domestic and foreign objects. This committee should convene with the industrial sector of this city to select specialized or responsible personnel to go for reference, and also take the opportunity to go to Shanghai to inspect the safety and sanitation facilities of major factories to learn from them. If possible, they will also contact the ministry to transport the collected items to Qingdao for exhibition in order to arouse widespread attention. Organization: The committee will select three members from among specialized personnel and appoint several technical staff from each industry to form an observation group, named the Qingdao Industrial Safety and Sanitation Inspection Group. The group will have a leader, a deputy leader, a document officer, an accountant, and a liaison officer. The leader will be designated by the Social Affairs Bureau from among the group members, and the deputy leader, document officer, accountant, and liaison officer will be mutually elected by the group members. The leader is fully responsible for directing the group's affairs. Activities: In order to gather ideas, the leader should convene group meetings at any time. The observation methods and schedule will be formulated by the leader and submitted to the group meeting for approval and implementation, and reported to the committee for forwarding to the Social Affairs Bureau for record. After the observation is completed, the leader and deputy leader should prepare a detailed report and send it to the committee for review. Expenses: The round trip is limited to two weeks, approximately sixteen days, three days in Beijing, and five days on the way. The cost of travel, accommodation, meals, and miscellaneous expenses is limited to 98 yuan per person, which will be borne by the organization represented by the group member. (26th)

Songjiang

A Patrol Officer Resigns After a Robbery in His Jurisdiction

Wang Shougen's rice store, located at No. 10, Jia 12, Bao 4, Aimin Town, Section 1 of the county, was suddenly attacked by six bandits around 9:00 PM the night before. Four bandits entered the store, while two stood guard outside. The bandits robbed the store of gold jewelry, cash, and other items, resulting in a loss of 200 yuan. When the victim's aunt, Jiang, shouted for help, the bandits angrily slashed her forehead with an axe, causing profuse bleeding. Subsequently, the local security, water, and land public security organs searched everywhere for the bandits but were unable to apprehend them by dawn. The next day, County Magistrate Li learned of the incident and considered it a serious oversight in defense that a robbery had occurred in the center of the area, injuring the victim. He ordered that the case be solved and the stolen goods and bandits be apprehended within three days. Failure to comply would result in the dismissal and punishment of the patrol officer and the responsible watch post. An emergency meeting was also convened. It is reported that the Aimin Town winter defense watch post has ordered the town mayor to establish it within three days and has dispatched a security team to station at Luo Shen Temple to deter criminals. However, Huang Heqing, the patrol officer in charge, has taken responsibility for the incident and submitted his resignation to the bureau chief.

Suzhou

Farmers Petition for Rent Reduction Dispute

Farmers in Xietang Township, due to the severe crop disaster this year, were very dissatisfied with the color requirements for rent collection by the owners of various businesses. Therefore, they watched and waited to return the rent, resulting in a small number of collections by various businesses. They requested the Public Security Bureau to strictly pursue the field rent. The day before yesterday, more than 1,000 farmers petitioned the Xietang Township District Office, demanding rent reduction. Director Zhang of the Public Security Bureau specially dispatched two branch directors, Huang Tian, to Xietang and other townships to urge rent collection. On the 25th, more than 1,000 farmers petitioned the district office for the second time, demanding rent reduction. Branch Director Huang immediately advised the farmers to return the rent, but the farmers did not listen and were tough in their attitude. Huang immediately ordered two rows of warning shots to be fired and arrested four stubborn tenants, including Zhang Yunxiang. Later, after mediation by township heads and others, the farmers dispersed. The next day, township heads convened an emergency meeting and resolved: Township Baojia chiefs should work with the Public Security Bureau to persuade farmers to return the rent as soon as possible and not blindly follow others. This year's disaster is severe, please ask the county to order various businesses to specify colors and reduce the length by 10%. Tenants should pay rent with rice. Please ask the owners to send people to the countryside to collect rent. Please ask the county to set up agricultural warehouses to provide relief. The above resolution will be delivered by Branch Director Huang to County Magistrate Wu on the 27th, and County Magistrate Wu will convene various owners to discuss the plan.

Wuxi

Security Teams from Eight Counties Inspected Yesterday

The security teams from eight counties in the second district of Jiangsu Province gathered in Wuxi for inspection. Inspection officers Yang Jingzhi, Meng Daozheng, Chen Fudian, Zhang Shaorao, Yuan Zhaodao, Chen Zuoyuan, Ma Jiren, Zhang Jiasheng, Ma Wei, Huang Zhichao, and Sun Fanwu arrived in Wuxi on the 25th. The next day, they went to Huishan to inspect internal affairs of various troops in groups. At 9:00 AM yesterday, the security teams from eight counties including Wuxi, Wujin, Wuxian, Wujiang, Changshu, Jiangyin, Kunshan, and Taicang, led by the brigade commander, departed to the training ground of the Provincial Education College in Sheqiao for a formal inspection. A military parade was held, and Inspection Officer Yang delivered a speech on behalf of Chairman Chiang, with many earnest words.

Changzhou

Zhencheng Road Uses Charcoal Vehicles

In order to prevent the outflow of profit rights on Su Province Zhencheng Road, it was decided to switch to charcoal vehicles. Six vehicles were transported to Shanghai for installation. On the 26th, four vehicles were driven from Shanghai to Changzhou, having been properly installed and tested with good results. The speed is 30 kilometers per hour. Since charcoal has not yet been transported to Changzhou, the date of charcoal vehicle operation has been decided to begin on the first day of the next year.

Nantong

Province Sends Personnel to Lecture Students

Students from Nantong College went to Beijing to petition, and the local authorities tried to dissuade them. The students were very determined and remained on the Dasheng Port Daiwa Wheel, refusing to return to school. On the 27th, the special office telegraphed Nantong College, saying that it had received a telegram from Chairman Chen of the Provincial Government, saying that students from Nantong College were going to Beijing to petition. Please supervise with the county magistrate and principal to strictly stop them and not let them leave the country, and order them to comply. It was also found that the students gathered at Dasheng Port and strongly occupied the ship, which was somewhat excessive. The office reported to the authorities and dispatched Secretary Sheng Shijie and Chief of Staff Peng Longxiang to dissuade them together with County Magistrate Jin Zonghua. In addition to the detention of the ship and suspension of dispatch, the telegram was specially sent to the college to quickly order the students to return to school. Also, the Provincial Government telegraphed Commissioner Xu to send personnel to Nantong to lecture and ask the students to return to school for classes.

Yangzhou

Students Stop Going to Beijing to Petition

The national salvation movement of students in Yangzhou City, with the provincial and private secondary schools as the center, originally had a proposal for provincial middle school students to send representatives to Beijing to petition. The Provincial Government Education and Construction Department sent Inspector Wu, Section Chief Xiang, Secretaries Zhou Xiang and Dai, and others to Yangzhou one after another to earnestly persuade them together with County Magistrate Ma Zhenbang, and the previous proposal has been withdrawn. It has been decided to issue national salvation publications, raise funds to relieve the medical expenses of injured students in Peiping, and organize rural lecture teams to carry out practical national salvation work.

Hangzhou

Qianjiang Bridge Hastens Pier Construction

The Qiantang River Bridge project is progressing actively and rapidly due to the winter dry season. The approach bridges on both banks are progressing smoothly. Seven of the ten approach bridge piers on the north bank have been completed. The base of the pier on the riverbank is about to be completed. The caissons used for the first and second piers are already more than 30 feet deep. The piers of the two highway bridges on the south bank have also been completed recently. Piling work is currently underway inside the steel sheet pile cofferdam of the riverbank approach bridge pier. Iron ships are being used day and night to speed up the piling work on the foundation of the main bridge. It is planned to increase the number of engine ships to increase efficiency. If there are no accidents, the entire project can be completed by the end of next year.

Hangzhou-Ningbo Plans to Establish Juvenile Prisons 99

The Zhejiang Higher Court believes that the current system in various prisons, which treats juvenile and adult offenders equally, is not appropriate. The physiology and psychology of juveniles and adults, and the motives and circumstances of crimes, are very different. It is necessary to establish separate juvenile prisons to specifically detain juvenile offenders under the age of 20. Following an order from the Ministry, it is instructed to refer to the Shandong method and first establish them in the provincial capital and major commercial ports. Preparations have begun to establish one in Hangzhou and Ningbo each, and then gradually expand.

Opening of Tianmu Mountain Sightseeing Train 100

The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Administration believes that Tianmu Mountain has magnificent scenery and has always been a scenic spot. At the time of snow and severe cold, the silver mountain and snow sea are even more beautiful. In order to facilitate people from all walks of life to enjoy the New Year holiday, a Tianmu Mountain sightseeing train will be organized from New Year's Day to the 3rd of January. Departures will be at 7:00 AM and return to Hangzhou at 6:00 PM. Round-trip fares can be negotiated with the bureau's sales office.

The Yuhuan County Government, following orders, is handling the training of township heads. More than 60 township heads were convened at the county government for training on the 15th. Training was held from 8:00 AM to 5:00 PM every day. Lunch was provided by the county government. The commencement ceremony for the winter national labor service county project in Yin County was held at 9:00 AM on the 24th at Beiguo Temple in the northern suburbs of this city. More than 3,000 people, including staff from various agencies and militia teams from the western and northern suburbs, attended. After the ceremony, they marched to the construction site. At 11:00 AM, Commissioner Zhao, Commander Wang, Standing Committee Member Wu, Director Yu, and County Magistrate Chen broke ground and participated in digging and carrying soil. Education Broadcasting Special Edition - Mandarin Lectures - What to Write 102

— Edited by Ye Shaojun of Kaiming Bookstore

Fellow students, the subject of Chinese involves many things. I won't talk about too many things, just a little about writing, divided into two parts. Today's topic is "What to Write," and the next topic is "How to Write." My words may not be of direct help to you, that is, your writing ability may not necessarily increase much after listening to my words. My words may be of some indirect help to you, that is, after listening to my words, pay attention to what should be paid attention to, avoid what should be avoided at any time, work hard in aspects that should be worked hard, and don't waste your mind in aspects that don't need attention. After a considerable amount of time, your writing ability will naturally gradually increase.

"When you start writing now, it can probably be divided into the following aspects: The Chinese teacher assigns topics on a regular basis for you to practice, and you have to write. After listening to various courses, sometimes you need to take notes; after doing various experiments, sometimes you need to write reports, and you have to write. After traveling to a place, you want to record what you have seen and heard, as well as your own feelings. When you are away from your family and relatives, you want to tell them about your recent life, and you have to write. Sometimes, from various perceptions, a kind of artistic conception is condensed, and you only feel that you must transform this kind of artistic conception into concrete words, either in the form of poetry or in the form of a novel or story, and then you feel happy, so you also have to write.

The writing materials in the above aspects are all original in your life, not forcibly taken from outside your life. In other words, these writing materials are all your own experiences. When we usually speak, from the extremely simple "Have you eaten?" and "This book is very good" to the extremely complex comments on a matter and speculations on a matter, it is all based on our own experiences. Because it is based on our own experiences, we can speak logically, without a single superfluous word or a single nonsensical word. If we go beyond the scope of our experience and talk nonsense, such as talking about how the stars move without any knowledge of astronomy, or trying to predict the future of the Italian-Ethiopian War and Japanese negotiations without any knowledge of international politics and economics, we will definitely say things that don't make sense and only provide people with material for ridicule. If a person has self-knowledge, he will never do such a stupid thing, talking nonsense beyond the scope of his own experience. He must know how much experience he has, in what aspects he can speak, and in what aspects he is not qualified to speak. It is not embarrassing to not speak in occasions where you are not qualified to speak, but rather a virtue of acting according to your ability and keeping within your limits. The scope of experience is like a ripple, expanding more and more. When it expands to a considerable extent, you are qualified to speak when you were originally not qualified, then speak, and it is not too late. Writing is originally a continuation of speaking, so to remedy the poverty of speaking, we take up our pens to write in occasions where speaking cannot reach. Therefore, writing should naturally be the same as speaking, only taking things within the scope of experience as writing materials, and not forcibly dragging things outside the scope of experience to the tip of the pen. Judging from the several aspects of writing that you are doing now, all writing materials are your own experiences, which is a very smooth thing. May you always follow this tendency, this is a flat and wide road.

The meaning of the previous layer seems very ordinary, but it is actually very important. Why? Because the attitude towards writing is established from this. Knowing that writing is originally a continuation of speaking, and that writing materials should be limited to one's own experience, this regards writing as an extremely ordinary but extremely serious matter. Everyone wants to write, just like everyone wants to speak, isn't it extremely ordinary? You cannot go beyond your own experience, you cannot be reckless, isn't it extremely serious? This attitude is normal. For people who hold this attitude, writing is a useful skill. There is also another attitude, regarding writing as an extremely special but extremely casual thing. This can be understood more clearly from the situation in the former private schools. In the past, there were many students in private schools, perhaps a dozen or so, or as few as three or four. These students did not all write articles. Those who were going to study engineering or commerce would be done after studying for a few years. Only a few who were preparing to take the imperial examination would start writing articles at a certain time. Starting to write articles was called "opening the pen," which was a great event. Students who opened their pens had to give the teacher extra tuition, and parents would say to others, "My child has 'opened the pen,'" often with a proud smile on their faces. Why was this? Because writing articles could be used to take the imperial examination, and future success all stemmed from this, so everyone regarded it as an extremely special thing, and this special thing belonged to a minority of people. Furthermore, what did they write after opening the pen? It was either "On Revisiting the Old to Know the New" or "On Emperor Gaozu of Han." They would turn over and over and entangle for a while and then finish the article. They would casually grab an event of Emperor Gaozu of Han, praise him or scold him, and that would be an excellent masterpiece. Especially if they praised what everyone scolded and scolded what everyone praised, this was called "reversing the case," and they could get a lot of praise from the teacher. Most of these materials were not their own experiences, but merely imitating the tone of others and piling up some irrelevant meanings. To put it bluntly, it was simply parroting and playing with words. Developing from this path, there came articles that specialized in piecing together allusions and poems that groaned without illness. One's own experience was like this, but what was written was not like this, perhaps it was even the opposite. Writing was divorced from real life and only became something to decorate life. What was the value of having this writing skill? Therefore, it is said that this attitude is extremely casual. Now, although the imperial examination has been abolished and writing starts as early as the first grade of elementary school, people's attitudes towards writing have not completely gotten rid of the old malady. Now every student has to write, which is certainly not a special thing for a minority of people, but we often hear students say, "I have no ideas, no materials, I simply can't write anything when I pick up a pen," or "We have to write again today, it's really annoying!" These words express a misunderstanding, thinking that writing is a special thing in school life, and that you have to leave your own experience to think of ideas and find materials. It seems that your own original experience is not worthy of being used as ideas or materials. Furthermore, inferring from here, it seems that the so-called ideas and materials are a kind of flowery words that sound very good and look very beautiful, but have no connection with real life. These flowery words must be searched for with great effort, like hunting dogs searching for birds and beasts lurking in the mountains and forests. You may not be able to get what you search for, so there are times when you can't write anything when you pick up a pen. Accumulating the experience of not being able to write anything for several times, you feel that writing is really an annoying thing. In fact, even if you can write something every time you write with this kind of attitude, it is not something to be happy about. Because writing, like speaking, is definitely not just writing some flowery words that sound very good and look very beautiful on paper and finishing it. It must be based on your own experience and flow out of real life, and that is in line with the original intention of writing articles. Like this, leaving your own experience and deliberately searching, although the effort of searching may be very troublesome, we cannot but say that he takes writing too casually. The attitude of seeing it as special and seeing it as casual makes writing a skill that is useless to life, so it must be changed. You might as well think for yourself: Do you regard writing as a special thing in school life? Do you deliberately search for empty materials away from your own experience? If you haven't, then that's the best. If you really do, and it's still like this today, then please change it immediately, change it to a normal attitude, which is to regard writing as ordinary and serious. People who hold a normal attitude will never say that they have no ideas or materials, because they will never have no experience, and experience is their ideas and materials. He will also never say that writing is really annoying, because writing is an item in his life, just like speaking and eating are items in life. No one will ever say that speaking and eating are really annoying. (To be continued)

Passenger and Freight Trains on Both Lines Fully Restored Yesterday Morning 103

General Order to Abolish Temporary Vehicle Scheduling Measures

Total Business Losses on Both Lines Approximately 300,000 Yuan

Traffic Resumes at the North Station, Police and Others Have Been Withdrawn

Students Petitioning in Beijing, After Earnest Persuasion by the Authorities, All Returned to Shanghai the Night Before Last, and Passenger and Freight Trains on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Lines Were Fully Restored Starting Yesterday Morning. Temporary Vehicle Scheduling Measures Were Abolished at the Same Time. Passenger and Freight Trains on Both Lines Have Fully Resumed

Xiao Weiguo, Director of the Train Operations Department, Went to Beijing to Report to the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Education Regarding the Details of the Obstruction of Passenger and Freight Trains on Both Lines Due to the Desire of Shanghai Students to Petition in Beijing. Starting at 6:00 AM, He Ordered the Sale of Tickets for the Beijing-Shanghai Line Heading North, the Fourth Shanghai-Beijing Express Train Departing from the North Station at 8:00 AM, and the Shanghai-Hangzhou Line Heading South, the Shanghai-Zhabei Express Train Departing from the North Station at 7:00 AM, and Other Passenger Tickets.

Representatives from Member Banks Such as Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Zhejiang Xingye Bank, South China Bank, National Credit Bank, Bank of Communications, China National Bank, Xinhua Bank, Jiangsu Silk Industry Bank, Siming Bank, Donglai Bank, Jiangsu-Zhejiang Bank, Hengli Bank, Kenye Bank, Juxingcheng Bank, Tonghe Bank, Yongheng Bank, China Remittance Bank, etc., Including Chen Guangfu, Song Ziliang, Tang Shoumin, Xu Jiqing, Bei Songsun, Luo Qinghua, Wang Zhixin, Chen Mutang, Qi Yunqing, Wu Weiru, Song Hanzhang, Pan Jiufen, Ye Fuxiao, Qu Jigang, Yang Jiemei, Wang Yansong, Lu Zidong, Qian Xinzhi, Hu Bijang, Wu Yunzhai, etc., 91 People in Total Attended. Secretary-General Lin Kanghou Was Present.

Reporting on Association Affairs At Around 4:00 PM, Chairman Chen Guangfu Announced That the Representatives of Each Bank Attending the Regular Meeting of Members Had Met the Legal Quorum and Immediately Opened the Meeting. Yuan Cheng'an Was in Charge of Recording. After Performing the Etiquette as Usual, the Chairman First Reported on the Progress of Handling Association Affairs in the Second Half of This Year. The Summary Is Recorded as Follows: Amending the Articles of Association of the Association, Requesting the Amendment of the Stamp Tax Law, Government Reform of the New Monetary Policy, Supporting the Promotion of Commercial Acceptance Drafts, Undertaking Disaster Relief Loans.

Passing Various Motions The Following Motions Were Discussed and Passed: Motion on the China Industrial Bank, China National Agricultural and Industrial Bank, China General Chamber of Commerce Bank, China Kenye Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Adding and Replacing Member Representatives, Resolved and Passed; Motion on the Sichuan Meifeng Bank, China Farmers Bank, Zhejiang Local Bank, Jiangsu Farmers Bank, Yongda Bank, and Pudong Bank Joining the Association, Resolved and Passed; Motion on the Final Accounts for the Second Half of This Year, Resolved and Passed; Motion on the Budget for the First Half of 1936, Resolved and Passed.

Amending Industry Regulations Article 3 of the Industry Regulations Regarding Holiday Dates Is as Follows (Banks That Usually Take Half-Day Holidays Must Report to the Association for Record). Because Each Bank Decided to Take Full-Day Holidays on Sundays Starting on New Year's Day Next Year, the Phrase "Banks That Usually Take Half-Day Holidays Must Report to the Association for Record" Was Deleted. Article 5 Was Changed to All Collections and Remittances Shall Comply with the Order of the Ministry of Finance on November 4, 1935, and Silver Coins Shall Be Used Generally. Article 11 Was Changed to "For Current Account Customers Who Withdraw Deposits by Check, Their Deposit Books (Receipt Slips) Should Be Stamped with the Bank's Receipt Stamp and Signed or Stamped by Important Staff Members as Proof." Article 7 "The Exchange Rate of Domestic Currency and Domestic and Foreign Exchange Rates Shall Be Determined and Published by the Association Daily" Was Deleted. The Meeting Adjourned at Around 5:00 PM.

Egg Merchants Request the Issuance of Public Bonds The Ministry of Finance Approved That It Should Be Unnecessary to Discuss 110

The Shanghai Egg Industry Association Said That in Recent Years, Various Countries in Southeast Asia and Europe and the United States Have Restricted the Import of Fresh Eggs from Our Country, Resulting in a Sharp Decline in Egg Exports and a Sharp Drop in Prices. Egg Merchants Are on the Verge of Danger. The Association Appealed to the Central Ministries and Courts, Requesting the Issuance of Egg Industry Public Bonds for Relief. The Executive Yuan Ordered the Ministry of Finance to Handle It. After Review by the Ministry of Finance, This Case Was Previously Reported to the Ministry by the Association. The Current Difficulties of the Egg Industry Are Indeed True. However, the Ministry Has Stipulated Ten Principles for Providing Relief to Shanghai Industry and Commerce, Specifically for Providing Relief to Shanghai Industry and Commerce. At the Time of Holding the Loan, If Each Manufacturer Complies with the Loan Principles, They Should Proceed Directly According to Legal Procedures. The Request to Issue Egg Industry Public Bonds Was Approved to Be Unnecessary to Discuss.

Tang Youren's Remains Encoffined Yesterday Afternoon 111

The French Concession Police Station Dispatched a Large Number of Detectives to Guard

Temporarily Placed in the Funeral Home and Will Be Buried After One Month

After Tang Youren, Vice Minister of Communications, Was Assassinated, His Remains Were Encoffined in the Shanghai Funeral Home in the Bitter Wind and Cold Rain Yesterday Afternoon at 2:00 PM. Hundreds of People from All Walks of Life Came to the Funeral to Offer Condolences. The French Concession Police Station Specially Dispatched a Large Number of Police Officers to Guard Around the Funeral Home. After the Encoffining, the Coffin Was Temporarily Placed in the Funeral Home. The Details Are Recorded as Follows:

Funeral Arrangement

Starting Yesterday Morning, the Funeral Committee Dispatched Personnel to Rush to Handle All Funeral Arrangements. Tang's Remains Were Moved to the Northernmost Center of the Hall. His Body Was Covered with Wreaths of Fresh Flowers, and His Face Was Covered with Red Silk. Those Who Paid Their Respects to His Remains Removed the Red Silk by Tang's Family Members. In Front of the Mourning Canopy Was a Photo of Tang, and the Front of the Case and the Four Walls of the Hall Were Filled with Wreaths and Elegies Presented by All Sectors. The Arrangement Was Solemn. On Both Sides of the Funeral Were Lounges for Male Guests, and Lounges for Female Guests Were Upstairs. Male Attendants Welcomed Guests at the Door of the Hall, and Female Attendants Welcomed Guests in Front of the Mourning Canopy. The Military Band Dispatched by the Municipal Public Security Bureau Was on the West End of the Hall's Front Porch, and the East End Was the Place Where Mourners Signed Their Names. The Arrangement Was Well Organized.

Police Guard

Leaders from All Walks of Life in China and Foreign Countries and Tang's Friends All Came to the Funeral to Offer Condolences During the Encoffining. Geng Jiaji, Secretary of the Municipal Government, and Zhou Jue, Director of the Diplomatic Ministry's Shanghai Office, Specially Went to the French Concession Police Station in Advance, Requesting the Dispatch of a Large Number of Police Officers to Guard Around the Shanghai Funeral Home. Therefore, the French Concession Police Station Specially Dispatched a Large Number of Police Officers to Guard Inside and Outside the Funeral Home Yesterday Afternoon. The Municipal Public Security Bureau Also Dispatched Police Officers to Guard Inside the Funeral Home.

Visiting Guests

Two to Three Hundred Leaders from All Walks of Life in China and Foreign Countries and Tang's Friends Came to Offer Condolences at the Encoffining, Including Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, Chen Shaokuan, Minister of the Navy, Zhang Qun's Wife, Representative of Zhang Qun, Minister of Foreign Affairs, Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, Huang Fu, Former Minister of the Interior, Liu Weichi, Director of the Ministry of Industry, Chen Jie, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, Xu Kan, Vice Minister of Finance, Kao Minyi, Xiao Tongzi, Wu Kaixian, Cai Jingjun, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Gan Hailan, Representative of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Zhou Yu, Director of the Diplomatic Ministry's Shanghai Office, Wang Changchun, Commissioner of the Municipal Government, Ling Gonghan, Director of the International Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Wen Yuqing, Director of the International Telecommunications Bureau, Huang Boqiao, Director of the Two Railways Administration, Bankers Chen Guangfu, Chen Xing, Xu Jiqing, Qian Xinzhi, Song Hanzhang, Hu Bijang, Bei Songsun, Celebrities Mei Lanfang, etc., as Well as Japanese Ambassador to China Arima, Counselor Horinouchi, Arino, Military Attaché Major General Isogaya, Lieutenant General Sato, Japanese Consul General in Shanghai Ishisa, Consul General in Beijing Suma, All Naval Officers in Shanghai, Polish Envoy to China Weidenthal, French Consul in Shanghai Gao Fa, etc., Were Often Led by Funeral Committee Attendants to the Funeral to Pay Their Respects.

Encoffined at 2:00 PM

Wearing Formal Attire in the Coffin, the Funeral Home Staff Carried Out the Rituals According to Convention. However, Tang Was from Hunan, According to Hunan Customs, the Rite of Holding Rice in the Mouth Should Be Performed Before Encoffining. The Rite Was Very Simple, Only the Master of Ceremonies Read a Few Sentences of the Words of the Rite of Holding Rice in the Mouth, and Tang's Children Knelt Before the Funeral. Then Encoffining Immediately Took Place. Tang's Elder Brother Guiliang, Younger Brother Bunian, Younger Sister Weishu, Wife Ouyang, and Two Sons and Two Daughters All Came to the Coffin. When Encoffining, Tang's Siblings Were in Great Grief, and Tang's Wife Especially Cried and Fainted Beside the Coffin. Although the Two Sons and Two Daughters Were Still Young, They Also Watched the Encoffining with Tears and Wiped Away Tears with Towels Frequently. Mourners Beside Them Were Also Saddened by This.

Temporarily Placed in the Funeral Home

After the Encoffining, Chen Jie, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, Offered Sacrifices on Behalf of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Visiting Guests Also Bowed Three Times. After the Ceremony Was Completed, They All Left the Funeral Home with Grief. The Remains Were Temporarily Placed in the Shanghai Funeral Home and Will Be Buried After One Month at a Selected Location. The Location Has Not Yet Been Decided.

Condolence Messages Continue to Arrive

Condolence Messages from All Parties Have Arrived in Shanghai One After Another. The Funeral Committee Received Several More Condolence Messages Yesterday Morning: President Dai of the Examination Yuan Wired, "Shocked to Hear of the Death of Brother Youren from Assassination, I am Extremely Saddened. It is a Pity for the Country That His Talent Was Not Fulfilled. I Hope You Will Restrain Your Grief. Dai Chuanxian Bows, Thanks." Director Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industry Wired, "Shocked to Hear of the Death of Mr. Youren from Assassination, I Am Deeply Saddened. I Send This Telegram to Offer My Condolences, Wu Dingchang Bows, Thanks." Chen Shuren, Chairman of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, Wired, "Upon Receiving the News That Vice Minister Tang Was Wounded by Assassination and Died, I Am Deeply Saddened. I Hope You Will Convey to Mrs. Tang My Condolences and Hope She Will Change and Restrain Her Grief, I Am Anxious, Chen Shuren Thanks."

Reward for Arresting the Murderer

Mayor Wu Tiecheng of This City Said That the Thugs Dared to Assassinate Vice Minister of Communications Tang Youren and Escaped Without a Trace, Which Is Extremely Illegal. Yesterday, He Specially Ordered the Municipal Public Security Bureau to Offer a Reward of 10,000 Yuan to Arrest the Murderer Within a Time Limit and Bring Him to Justice. He Also Sent Letters to the Police Authorities of the Public Concession and the French Concession, Asking Them to Assist in the Investigation and Arrest.

Eurasia Airlines Leases Giant Aircraft, Expected to Arrive in Shanghai Today 112

Landing at Longhua at 3 PM

If Weather is Bad, Will Remain in Guangzhou

According to the Guowen News Agency, Eurasia Airlines' newly leased Junkers-style third trimotor giant aircraft from German Lufthansa, piloted by the renowned German aviator Gu Rug, co-piloted by Du Xu, and with telegrapher Qu Luosi and mechanic Bu Erluo, departed Berlin on the 20th of this month to fly to China. According to inquiries made by reporters to the company yesterday, the aircraft had already flown from Hanoi to Guangzhou yesterday morning. If the weather is clear, it will fly from Guangzhou to Shanghai this morning and is expected to arrive and land at Longhua at 3 PM this afternoon. If the weather is bad, the company may send a telegram requesting that it remain temporarily in Guangzhou. As for the aircraft's design, speed, and safety equipment, it is exactly the same as the two previously leased aircraft. Upon arrival in Shanghai, it will immediately join the Shanghai-Xinjiang-Shaanxi-Chengdu routes. To express its welcome, the company specially dispatched He En, the agent of the air navigation group, to Guangzhou yesterday morning to guide it to Shanghai.

Overseas Silver Prices Plummet, Three Banks Strive to Stabilize Foreign Exchange, Foreign Exchange Selling Prices Still at Standard Levels, but Balancing Tax Rates Have Fallen Accordingly 113

Since the disastrous fall in overseas silver prices, foreign banks, finding no profit, have restricted the buying and selling of foreign exchange. The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, in order to stabilize foreign exchange, have continued to buy and sell foreign exchange without restrictions. As a result, the foreign exchange trading of these three banks has suddenly flourished. Fortunately, through strenuous efforts to stabilize it, the daily announced telegraphic transfer selling prices remain at standard levels, but the balancing tax rate, due to the continued decline in overseas silver prices, has also fallen accordingly. Yesterday, the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee announced a balancing tax rate of 10.5 percent. The Central Bank announced telegraphic transfer selling prices of one shilling and two and a half pence for one national currency in London, US$29.75 for one hundred national currency in New York, 452 francs for one hundred national currency in Paris, 73.75 marks for one hundred national currency in Berlin, 103 yen for one hundred national currency in Japan, and 93 Hong Kong dollars for one hundred national currency in Hong Kong.
