Chunqiu (Annals)

Preface to "Notes on What I Saw" 208

The vast world is originally an enlarged kaleidoscope. As long as you open your eyes to look, you can see all kinds of colors and bizarre sights, often beyond your expectations. Every strange thing, before you have witnessed it with your own eyes, you always think it will never happen; who knows that once you see it, this will happen, which makes you exclaim strangely. In the city, there are many people, and strange things are constantly evolving there. We coldly watch, which is the most meaningful. Whether it's a scale, a claw, or a fragment, they all have value for your observation and recording, so you can see people's hearts, and see the world change, and make scholars who study society get some reference materials. This magazine recently opened a new column "Notes on What I Saw", which is what it means. Unexpectedly, for two weeks, contributors have been pouring in, and it is impossible to publish them all. Well, let's publish a special page.

Notes on What I Saw (1) 209

— Shouqiu

Outside Shuixi Gate in the capital, there is a large stone bridge, and there are many children in ragged clothes at both ends of the bridge. These children stand at both ends of the bridge all day long, because they also have their expectations. What are their expectations? That is to wait for the small vendors carrying baskets and the coal deliverymen pushing handcarts to cross the bridge, so that they can steal from them, even rob openly.

One afternoon, I saw with my own eyes a woman carrying a basket selling eggs. These children stole a lot of eggs, because their stealing skills are very clever, so the woman didn't realize it. It wasn't until passers-by told her that more than twenty eggs had been stolen from the basket! The woman's capital was at stake, and she couldn't help crying loudly!

This phenomenon seems to be an important issue in society, right? I hope the police authorities pay attention to it.

Notes on What I Saw (2) 210

— Xufeng

Last year, I once sailed the sea. The sea was vast, and I saw many flying fish.

Flying fish can leave the water and fly, probably as a special way to avoid enemies. It is said that there are large fish in the water that want to eat flying fish, so I have seen dozens of fleeing flying fish fly out of the water, use their tails to propel themselves in the water, and leap into the air. A pair of pectoral fins, almost the same length as the body, spread out like wings, supporting the body to make three or four wave-like movements in the air, and then return to the water more than ten feet away from the starting point?

Ah! Unfortunate flying fish, although flying in the air to avoid strong enemies in the water, but there are also groups of gulls and crows in the air, waiting eagerly. Therefore, I have also seen several flying fish sacrificed. The weak in the world really have no happy land anywhere!

Notes on What I Saw (3) 211

— Xu Xiaoting

In the cold winter morning, our Xinghua people's habit is that after getting up every day, for washing faces, gargling, drinking tea, etc., we need hot water, and hot water must be bought from the tea stove. The tea stove burns reed grass, and rice husks. The colder the weather, the colder the water, and it can't be boiled quickly. More and more people gather. Wherever there is a tea stove in the streets and alleys, it is always lively and crowded. The cold wind is blowing, and the cold is piercing. To seek heat (water), you must first suffer the cold. A group of friends who buy hot water are shrinking their necks, stretching their heads, their hands and feet are cold, and they are looking eagerly. This can really leave a microcosm for those who are enthusiastic. The more you look at it with a hot heart, the more you will be splashed with a basin of cold water, which makes you uneven in hot and cold, and you really don't know whether to laugh or cry.

Leisurely and Contented! 212

Notes on What I Saw (4) 213

— Huang Lian

Yesterday, our Si'an city was performing "rewarding the gods opera"!

On the stage, I saw a young modern woman from another place, holding a small dog in her hand!

Next to the theater, there was a food stall selling beef vermicelli. I saw the woman throwing pieces of beef from the stall into the dog's mouth!

Finally, the woman took out a two-corner auxiliary currency note from her leather bag and left.

At this time, the two beggars sitting on the ground looked at it with envy! So they chased after her and begged: "Miss! Do a good deed!" But they got nothing!

Notes on What I Saw (5) 214

— Li Qing

Time: 4:52 PM on a certain day in December.

Location: National Loan Company.

A handsome middle-aged man was selecting woolen undershirts on the south-facing cabinet. He was wearing a gabardine coat, a blue-gray woolen hat, and satin small round-mouth shoes. Although he couldn't be called "a man of outstanding appearance," he was still a man of property.

But he started stealing things. He took advantage of the gap to stuff a soft, snow-white woolen undershirt into his coat pocket. Unexpectedly, the attempt failed, and a clerk spotted him. So several people rushed forward, twisting and roaring, and the rest of the clerks also shouted and cheered, shouting "Catch the thief!"

He stammered, unable to speak, only mumbling vaguely:

"I want to buy it, I want to buy it..."

But he was finally twisted into the manager's office by a clerk.

I thought silently: Beautiful people are smart, and evil deeds are also the work of smart people.

Notes on What I Saw (6) 215

— Jiachensheng

In public buses or trams, men and women giving up their seats is almost a common sight and nothing rare.

Giving up seats was originally a Western custom. Our noble compatriots are full of arrogance and imitative nature. Giving up seats is a virtue. Being able to imitate is certainly not a bad thing.

However, if we examine these seat-givers more carefully, the seats they give up are all given to modern girls. No matter how unsteady the old ladies are, no one will be polite. Situations like this can be seen anytime and anywhere. The virtue of giving up seats, perhaps should be like this for fashionable people. What a strange thing!

Notes on What I Saw (7) 216

— Yingdai

The day before yesterday, I went to the zoo and saw a woman on Wenmiao Road strip a child under one year old naked, hide him in her chest, and kneel on the ground crying. People who passed by gave her copper coins, pitying the child blowing in the wind naked. On our road, there is often a young beggar carrying an eighty-year-old mother on his back, with gray hair and a sack over her, shouting "My old mother" and begging. Everyone will give him money, pitying his old mother. The former uses the child, and the latter uses the old mother. Isn't the young woman and the strong man both good at doing work and doing small business to support the child and the old mother? However, it is always easier and less laborious to use the old and the young to beg for money.

Notes on What I Saw (8) 217

— Zuichiao

When Guangxi Road reaches 8 o'clock in the evening, a large public food stall will rest on the sidewalk. Many coolies and rickshaw pullers will come together to buy a few copper coins' worth of rice, and he will buy a few copper coins' worth of porridge. Side dishes are free and don't cost money. So that group of hungry people surround and eat, and with full bellies, they fight with the bad environment again; indeed, this public food stall is their only merciful God!

On a rainy night yesterday, they were still eating in the open air as usual. An officer came from afar with his chest out and his belly protruding, and his solemn face was enough to make them shudder! "Damn, go away, go into the lane, foreigners don't allow selling," the food stall owner almost cried, begging repeatedly: "Spare me, small business is very troubled"! "Damn, no, go into the lane!" The stronger person roared: Those coolies and rickshaw pullers came to plead together: "Please let him go; otherwise, we will have to go hungry, please do a good deed," The food stall owner, with a mournful face, trembling throat, snatched the rope on his shoulders, and said, "If their bellies are full, my family will be full! Spare me one cut"!

I finally couldn't bear to look at this tragedy; and the officer roared like a tiger, "Go away! What are you looking at"? But I think I can vaguely understand these fragments, in Chinese territory, Chinese people can't do business? It's common for Chinese people to bully each other in China, but it's strange to say foreign territory in his mouth! Who said the city is civilized? It's simply a beast that doesn't understand humanity!

Notes on What I Saw (9) 218

— Xianweisheng

The night before last, after dinner, I was idle and had nothing to do, so I went to the streets with Zhou Zihuan Yu and Xu Zibojian. While talking and walking, when we walked close to Linping Road in Hongkou, we saw a very large red and green "cloth windshield" in front of a north-facing shop, shaking in the wind.

Looking closer, it was a "Huguan Noodle Shop". How strange! The "cloth windshield" was made of the "national flag". The "Blue Sky" and "White Sun" were also complete, and the "Red Earth" was not missing at all, but the color was slightly darker.

I didn't see it, but when I saw it, I was heartbroken! Because I thought of how much foreigners "respect" the "national flag"? In the movies, sometimes when they encounter the national flag, they stand up to "salute". We Chinese people, not to mention saluting the national flag, are now using it as a windshield. Foreigners are afraid of laughing secretly behind their backs when they see it.

Notes on What I Saw: "Yi Ya Reborn" 219

— Banleng

A tooth-setting shop outside the South Gate of Dinghai hangs a sign that says: "Yi Ya Reborn". Note: Yi Ya was a temple person of Duke Huan of Qi in the Spring and Autumn Period. He was favored for his cooking taste. There is a saying: "Duke Huan of Qi was not happy in the middle of the night, and Yi Ya fried and grilled and presented it, and Duke Huan ate it and was full." Now, calling a tooth-setting person "Yi Ya Reborn" is a literal translation that makes people laugh when they see it.

Record of Observations 10 220

— Wang Shapa

Every time I stroll along the road, I often see the laborers on cargo trucks teasing women walking along the streets, either spitting or throwing mud, taking advantage of their lack of preparedness to commit mischief at will. If you try to reason with them, their truck has already driven far away.

Today, while returning home from buying things on the street, I passed Jisi Feier Road. Near the entrance of the zoo in Fanwangdu Park, I saw a cargo truck loaded with bricks pass by. The laborers on the truck were grinning and said to two girls walking along the street, "Hey! Sister, I'll come to your house at night!" But the two girls just lowered their heads and didn't say anything.

I thought to myself: These laborers' actions, whether spitting, throwing mud, or saying vulgar words, are ultimately a manifestation of the lack of education and knowledge among our Chinese people due to the lack of universal education.

Record of Observations: A Compromise 221

— Bai Kou

Yesterday afternoon, because I didn't have any homework, I took the opportunity to go to the Peiping Library. After taking a seat, I routinely looked around. As a result, I saw an old man sitting by the window, about sixty years old, wearing a long gown and mandarin jacket, with thick glasses. In front of him was a thread-bound woodblock book, and he was concentrating on reading it. Sitting next to him was a young woman, lightly powdered, wearing a fur coat, exuding a modern aura. In front of her was a foreign original book, and she was also reading it with great interest. The disharmonious situation between the two of them seemed to symbolize something about to happen.

In the first few minutes, everyone was at peace. Later, the young woman suddenly left her seat and walked straight to the window, opening the closed window with a bang. Although she didn't announce the reason for opening the window, I guessed that it was probably because she was wearing too warm clothes and wanted to cool off with the wind, or because the air in the room was not fresh enough and she wanted to open the window to change the air. In short, no matter what her reason for opening the window was, as soon as the window was opened, the cold wind immediately rushed in from the window. The old man began to shiver, and his concentration on reading could no longer be maintained. So he slowly got up and closed the window. His reason for closing the window was obviously because he was afraid of the cold. When the young woman sitting next to him saw this, she immediately stood up, walked to the window, and opened the window again. Judging from the expression on her face, she was a little angry, as if to say, "You old fellow, how dare you oppose me!" When the old man saw that the window was open again, obviously conflicting with his own interests too seriously, he couldn't help but feel angry, so he closed the window again, showing that the weak also have the spirit of resistance. When the young woman saw this, she immediately stood up, walked to the window, and slammed the window open again. Her steps were heavier than before, and her actions were more violent, obviously angry. When the old man saw this, he didn't show weakness either, and immediately closed the window with a thud, showing the spirit of being old but vigorous. When the young woman saw this, she was simply furious, and immediately opened the window again. When the old man saw this, he got up and closed it again. This opening and closing continued, but what was strange was that although the expressions on their faces showed that they were irreconcilable, they remained silent and quietly continued their work of opening and closing. I watched from the side and couldn't help but find it funny, but for my own benefit, I wanted to stand on the old man's side and join the battle. But then I thought, the old man wants to close the window because he is afraid of the cold, and it would be too ridiculous for someone as young as me to be afraid of the cold. As a result, I adopted a neutral attitude. Their work of opening and closing continued. If it weren't for the librarian to mediate, I'm afraid it would still be going on. Because neither side would give in, the librarian found it difficult to mediate. Later, he proposed a compromise: "The window should be half-open and half-closed." A storm was finally stopped. But the cold wind continued to come in from the half-open window, and the old man continued to shiver. The readers who had no vested interests watched from the sidelines from beginning to end, and no one was willing to express a fair opinion. So I couldn't help but sigh and say, "With compromise, the weak always suffer."

Record of Observations: Loss 222

— Qi Zhong

When things are lost, what is lost must be objects, and they must be things that are carried around, such as pens, books, wallets, watches, handkerchiefs, etc. If these things are lost while they are placed somewhere, then it is theft, and it cannot be called a loss. If an animal is lost and it is called a loss, that's a joke!

On Jiayu Road, I saw a red-paper "Looking for a Horse" advertisement posted on a utility pole, saying that a horse was lost. I felt that the gentleman who wrote the advertisement must not have a very clear understanding of literature, so he couldn't distinguish between "loss" and going missing. Unexpectedly, coincidentally, on the 6th, a Shanghai newspaper had a headline in the news: "Li Zibin is Looking for a Lost Girl." I don't know if Mr. Li's girl is made of stone or wood, lost in a pocket? Or lost with other things under his arm? If it is a living animal, then it is either missing or abducted. Calling it a loss doesn't seem quite right!

Special Article

The Chinese Tea Industry (3) 236

— Baiyi

Java was originally a market for Chinese tea, as mentioned earlier. However, in 1934, the export of Chinese tea to the islands of Java and Madura was only 82,580 kilograms, worth only 89,124 guilders. During the same period, the import of Japanese and Taiwanese tea to Java reached 1,449,051 kilograms, worth 1,452,201 guilders, far exceeding the export of Chinese tea to Java. In 1933, Chinese tea exports to Java were still 210,000 kilograms, worth 230,000 guilders, but in just one year, there was a sharp decrease of about two-thirds. The main reason for the rapid decline in Chinese tea exports to Java is the sharp increase in tea production in Java itself, but the large-scale import of Japanese and Taiwanese tea indicates that there are other factors involved. What are these factors? The exchange rate.

North Africa was originally a market for Chinese green tea, but since 1930, it has also been penetrated by Japanese green tea. In 1928, the Central Association of Japanese Tea Industry Organizations, in order to develop the sales channels for green tea, sent Mr. Sakuku Torii to the Philippines to promote it. In 1929, there was an export of 1,098 pounds, but this was only for samples. The following year, exports increased to 14,000 pounds. By 1931, exports increased sharply to 4,180,000 pounds. In 1932, the increase was even greater, reaching 11,650,000 pounds. In 1932, the increase was about 25 times greater than in 1931. The methods used by Japan are worth noting. When Japan exported green tea to Morocco in 1910, its quality was far inferior to Chinese tea and did not meet the needs of the local market. Therefore, it was often mixed with about three-sevenths or four-sixths of Chinese tea and sold under Chinese tea names. However, in the following year, due to improvements in its form and quality, Japanese green tea was able to develop independently. That year, it accounted for 20% of the total import volume in Morocco. At the same time, its price was lower than that of Chinese tea, with each pound being one to ten pence cheaper. The above is the direct reason for the loss and narrowing of the Chinese tea market.

4. The Technological Backwardness of the Chinese Tea Industry

The competition between emerging tea-producing countries and China has been described above. However, due to its geographical location, the quality of Chinese tea is the best in the world. Why is it that it is not as good as the later comers like Ceylon, Japan, India, and Java, and has been eroded in its traditional Chinese tea market? The reasons: First, the value of Chinese currency is controlled by the major world powers. At a time when currency inflation is widespread in the world, China's exchange rate has lost its balance, resulting in a general lack of improvement in foreign trade. Because China is on the silver standard, and the major world powers are on the gold standard, the silver used in China is regarded as a commodity in the gold standard countries. Therefore, when the price of gold increases, the price of silver decreases, and vice versa. The major world powers, for their own sake, demand the development of export trade and implement currency devaluation policies. As a result, the price of silver increases, and the market price of Chinese exports overseas also increases, and their sales naturally gradually decrease. Second, the technology of Chinese tea production has not yet reached the stage of improvement. Most of them still use the handicraft method of production. Therefore, in terms of quantity, it cannot be proportional to the production of emerging tea-producing countries. In terms of quality, it mostly maintains its original state. At the same time, the bad habits of merchants have not been eliminated, such as adding water to the tea to increase its weight and dyeing the tea to deceive consumers.

The former reason is not a problem of the tea itself, so there is no need to explain it here. In the future, I only hope that the central government authorities will work hard to balance international exchange rates with political power. The latter reason is the real problem of the current tea industry. Because if the problem of tea itself can be solved, then Chinese tea still has the hope of making a comeback in the world market.

In order to understand the current situation of the Chinese tea-making industry, I will briefly describe the famous tea-making situations in various places as follows:

(Anhui) Anhui is the richest area in China for tea production. According to the survey of the Department of Industry and Commerce of the Baoye Department: the total tea production in the province in 1920 was 293,700 dan. The method of making Qimen black tea in Anhui Province does not take advantage of sunlight, so the withering and fermentation are not very good. Because the temperature is too high, when brewing with boiling water, there is often a sun odor. At the same time, in recent years, tea farmers in Anhui Province have lengthened tea buds to six or seven inches due to the poor market conditions, and picked the stems and leaves together, only seeking quantity and not quality. Also, the method of making green tea in Anhui Province is to stir-fry the green in an iron pot, or to expose it to sunlight, so its color and fragrance are not good. The Anhui Provincial Government has recently established a model tea farm in Huoshan, imitating the Japanese method of making green tea. Machine-made tea. However, most of Anhui Province still uses hand-made tea.

(Zhejiang) Tea is produced in 75 counties in Zhejiang. According to the report of the Zhejiang Construction Department, the annual tea production in Zhejiang Province is about 200,000 dan. However, the method of making tea in Zhejiang Province still follows the old method. That is, the newly picked tea leaves are stir-fried in a pot, and when about one-tenth of the moisture is dried, they are taken out and placed on a bamboo curtain, rounded by hand, and re-stir-fried or placed in a baking cage to bake, and it is done. The method of making the famous Zhejiang tea Longjing tea is also the same, but it is slightly more precise.

(Jiangxi) The tea-producing area in Jiangxi reaches more than 50 counties. Gan tea has a long history of being sold overseas. According to tea merchants, about 190,000 boxes of Gan Ning black tea and about 200,000 boxes of flower tea were exported every year during the 31st and 32nd years of Guangxu, with a total of about 500,000 boxes in the province. It can be seen its prosperity. Later, under the influence of competition from foreign teas such as Ceylon and Indian tea, it gradually declined and fell into a slump. (To be continued)

Shenbao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

Amateur Talks

Realism and Futurism 237

— Changming

Grasping reality and paying attention to the future are, in general, the correct philosophy of life for us, and should not be a problem. The problem is how to grasp reality and pay attention to the future, what reality should be grasped, and what future should be paid attention to. Moreover, if we can properly grasp and pay attention to reality and the future, then the two are not completely contradictory and incompatible.

Grasping reality means that people should pay attention to the objective state of affairs that has already become a reality or is becoming a reality, and should pay attention to the immediate and practical interests that have appeared or can appear in ourselves, and should not deviate from the objective reality and practical interests and fall into fantasy and disillusionment. Paying attention to the future means that people should pay attention to the changes in objective things, establish our long-term goals by predicting their inevitable development, continue to be guided by new ideals, and create our new lives, instead of simply sticking to current interests or living and acting blindly. Indeed, people live in reality, and even more so in the current environment composed of current realities. If we leave the natural and social material realities and completely disregard the current practical interests, we will immediately not be able to survive. However, people do not live today and do not need to continue living tomorrow. Striving for tomorrow's survival has the same meaning and importance as striving for today's survival. Therefore, in today's survival, we should not only consider today and forget tomorrow. In order to prepare for tomorrow's survival, and even to survive more happily than today, it is absolutely necessary to foresee the future and establish a new ideal and goal for the future, and even strive purposefully for the future and strive for a new and long-term future. Therefore, if we talk about realism based on striving for today's survival, and futurism based on striving for tomorrow's survival, both are legitimate philosophies of life. And because people live today and will continue to live tomorrow, and today we must lay the foundation for tomorrow's survival, it is very right to talk about both realism and futurism at the same time.

However, this does not mean that all realism and futurism are correct and should be pursued. In fact, only realism that is based on the social and collective interests and does not abandon the ideal of moving towards a new life in the future, and futurism that can not be separated from the demands of the real world and striving for current survival, are worth adopting. In today's world, there are various incorrect tendencies in the pursuit of realism and futurism. In realism, some people pursue reality completely from the standpoint of individualism. As long as they can obtain benefits and power, that is, it is in their own realistic interests, they can disregard the interests of others, and even disregard the historical judgment of themselves in the future and the unfortunate fate that will eventually give them in the future, and blindly pursue their current gains. In addition, there are other people who just tell people to be content with their current lives and not to be dissatisfied with reality. As for the ideals of the future, in their view, they are absolutely empty fantasies. They only tell people to live blindly in history, so that everyone is completely isolated from the future. The former are individualistic and purely utilitarian realists, and the latter are conservative realists. But both of these are the same in that they are only satisfied with stopping at the pursuit of real life.

There is also an incorrect tendency towards the future. Some people completely abandon the pursuit of material life in the real world, and even leave the world of man, and only pursue the future or even the liberation of the soul after death. This is the futurism used by religious people to deceive and tempt the masses. Because they teach people to forget and endure all the pain of reality and oppose people's eagerness to fight for the improvement of real life. They believe that all happiness and rewards can be obtained in the future, in another future world after death: and the endurance of real pain is precisely the cause of creating good results in the future. This kind of futurism is a completely hopeless blank check, it only tells people to maintain the status quo.

From the perspective of common sense, it seems that reality and the future are two contradictory extremes, but in fact they are not contradictory, but rather complementary and interdependent. Because without the satisfaction of reality, the survival of mankind would be fundamentally shaken, and there would be no way to talk about future survival. If you can't survive today, how can you talk about continuing to survive tomorrow? So to be able to survive tomorrow, and to be able to survive better tomorrow, it must be conditioned on today's survival. This means that the future must be based on reality, and the future cannot be separated from reality. On the contrary, if we survive now, we will continue to survive in the future, and we must be able to survive better. Then mankind will have the consciousness of progress, and be in line with the consciousness of satisfying mankind's desire to move upward. Otherwise, mankind's way of surviving tomorrow will still only remain at the stage of today's way of surviving, and even if we survive today, we will no longer be able to continue to survive tomorrow. These are not the lives of human beings. Today's survival is a preparation for tomorrow's survival, so in today's survival, we must pre-exist the new requirements for tomorrow's survival, and must take the purpose and ideal of continuing to survive tomorrow. So the future survival is the continuation of the real survival, and without the future, reality is also meaningless.

Therefore, the correct philosophy of life is that it can allow people to pursue realism, and also allow people to pursue futurism at the same time, and does not regard the two as absolutely contradictory and incompatible things. However, we must exclude that realism centered on individual utilitarianism, and realism that does not pay attention to the future at all and has no new ideals of the future, and we must also exclude the futurism of religious worldly thoughts that does not talk about reality at all, or only tells people to endure the pain of reality, does not think about improvement, and only entrusts its sweet dreams to the future. Because these are the reasons that hinder the collective interests of mankind's real life and the life philosophy of mankind's progress.

Life

Silk Factory Apprentice 238

— Zhang Changban

I attended a national primary school in the village when I was young, but because my family was poor, I could not enter the higher primary school. So I left the study and went to the mountains to herd cattle and sheep. But this life did not last long before my father sent me to a silk factory in the city to be an apprentice. At that time, it was the end of the European War (I found out later), and the silk industry was particularly developed. Five or six new ones had opened just in our county. Because the number of factories increased, there was a need for many reserve silk craftsmen--apprentices. So, advertisements were posted in the city and in various rural towns to recruit apprentices, and I was one of the many people who applied and were accepted at that time.

The silk factory I entered had a long history. Because of the development of business, it had undergone an expansion, so the scale was also very grand. It was considered to be the best in our city. Inside, there were a total of 400 silk reeling machines, and there were also more than 700 craftsmen and apprentices. The first day I went there, I was very happy when I suddenly saw such a large house. People who were used to living in huts in the countryside, once they arrived here, it was like ascending from hell to heaven. So, I followed my father to the "Management Office." The head of management was a short, middle-aged man. He asked my father for my name and age, and after completing the "guarantee" formalities, he said to me sternly, "The rules of the factory are very strict. You are new here, so you must be extra careful." He immediately ordered the administrator standing next to him, "Take him to the 'Cocoon Sorting Area'."

I followed the administrator out of the management office in fear and trembling, and I didn't dare to express anything when I said goodbye to my father.

In the cocoon sorting area, there were already several apprentices who had entered the factory before me. They were still doing this basic preliminary work. I learned from them for less than twenty minutes, and then I knew that "double-ended cocoons," "suppurated cocoons," "moth-shell cocoons," "maggot cocoons," and "stained cocoons" were all bad things that could not be reeled into silk. This work was very simple and easy. As long as your eyes were sharp and your fingers were quick, you could be a good cocoon sorter.

It was not easy to wait until the "Cocoon Market" closed (after the new cocoons were launched on the market, the silk factory bought them in large quantities. Among them, many bad cocoons had to be sorted out, and then woven and dried for storage), and then the cocoon sorting work was completed. Naturally, I also knew that the other work was not necessarily easier than this, but changing the taste would always make people feel excited. Later, the same administrator who was there before took me to the "Reeling Area." This job was nothing special either. It was just transferring the silk from the "small spools" to the "large spools" of the "Reeling Machine." The reeling machine was very heavy, and several strong apprentices took turns using hand-cranked, like me, a "little kid," you only needed to pay attention to the silk strips, don't let them retreat over the reels, or connect the ends. When the silk strips on the big spools reached a certain amount, then put them on the silk drying rack, dry them, and then send them to the "Packing Area," and then the work was

Page 18

considered complete.

In the second year after I entered the factory, I was assigned to the "Silk Threading Area." This was considered to be the real contact with apprentice life. The silk threading area was divided into four areas: east, south, west, and north, arranged in a "口" shape. Each area had hundreds of silk reeling machines, and they were divided into four rows. Most of the silk threaders were craftsmen who had completed their apprenticeship, and a few were apprentices who were about to complete their apprenticeship. We little kids naturally did not have the qualification to "get on the machine." We could only serve five silk reeling machines for one person, helping the craftsmen to boil cocoons, change water, make fire, add charcoal, scoop out debris, or sweep the floor and send spools to the reeling area. It was really like a "stage extra" on the stage, throwing this away and changing that.

The factory stipulates that you have to get up at five o'clock every morning, but we always have to get up half an hour earlier to help the craftsmen boil the cocoons, add water to the silk pot, and make a fire. This way, we can win the craftsmen's favor, and at the same time, we can avoid being in a panic temporarily. Because the craftsmen make one or two more silk, they can get one or two more wages. If you delay his chance to make money, you will be scolded. The silk pot has to be changed three times a day, and each machine has to boil at least five portions of cocoons a day. At the same time, you have to add charcoal, scoop out debris, and send spools. The affairs of the five machines are all piled on one person, so we almost spend all day going back and forth between the machine rows, running from the silk reeling area to the cocoon boiling room, from the reeling area to the water storage pool. This craftsman is shouting, and that craftsman is shouting again. It is really very lively. At ten o'clock at night, the craftsmen clock out and go to bed, and we little apprentices still have to clean up the silk pots, sort out the debris, and sweep the floor. It will take at least half an hour before we can crawl into bed and sleep.

The place where we sleep is also called the "dormitory." Ten or more people sleep in the same room. To the left is the latrine, and to the right is connected to the "debris storage room." So, every summer season, plagues and diseases will be popular in the factory.

As for our meals, breakfast and lunch are both dry rice, and dinner is thin porridge. The so-called rice is white rice, but when you eat it, it has no rice taste, and it is so hard that you can't swallow it. At first, I didn't understand why this was. Later, I found out that the rice was soaked in lime water. This was a method devised by the kitchen in order to extract more profits and make people eat less rice.

Economic News

Recent Global Oil Market 239

— Fang Kuanren

Speaking solely from the perspective of market needs, the global oil market in recent years has indeed shown a slight increase in demand. The main reason for this is the increase in the production of automobiles, airplanes, and other industries in various countries. In fact, although the global automobile production volume continued to decrease in 1933, this decrease not only stopped in 1934, but also saw a significant increase. Although complete statistics for this year are not yet available, judging from the expansion of armaments in various countries and the automobile production situation in various countries in the past few months, it can be inferred that global automobile production is still increasing. According to statistics, the number of automobiles worldwide in 1934 was 34.9 million, an increase of 8% compared to 1933; also, the demand for gasoline in 1934 was 67.5 million tons, an increase of 6.9% compared to 1933.

According to the Berlin Business Cycle Research Institute, the registration index of newly manufactured light automobiles in the world's four major capitalist countries in the past two years is as follows:

1933 1934

United States 136.2 173.3

United Kingdom 119.7 148.3

France 108.1 111.5

Germany 199.5 318.4

(1932 == 100)

From this small table of statistics, it can also be seen that the automobile production of the world's four major capitalist countries has increased significantly in the past year. Among them, Germany has shown a surprising increase, which is naturally closely related to its efforts to expand armaments.

As for the increase in the number of airplanes in the world, it goes without saying that everyone is desperately expanding their air forces. However, since newspapers and magazines often have statistics on airplanes in various countries, we feel that there is no need to copy the statistics here again.

Logically, the increase in the production of automobiles and airplanes around the world, and the resulting increase in the demand for oil, should result in higher oil prices. However, the reality is the opposite of what is expected. Since last year, although the global demand for oil has increased with the increase in automobiles and airplanes, its price has shown a significant drop. According to what has been published this year, the prices of oil products worldwide in recent years are as follows:

Average Price (1929 == 100)

The sharp decline in global oil prices in recent years is clearly shown in this table. But what is the reason for the oil price drop? This is because: Firstly, the struggle among the world's trusts for the remaining oil resources and oil markets in the world is becoming increasingly acute. For example, in the struggle for Iraqi oil resources among the world's trusts last year, and in the struggle for Abyssinian oil resources among Britain, the United States, and Italy this year, ruthless and fierce struggles have been manifested. Also, the struggle between countries such as Britain and the United States for the world's oil market has also been developing at an accelerated pace in recent years. Secondly, the struggle for "oil independence" by general oil-consuming countries continues. This can be clearly seen in the efforts to develop domestic resources, the development of the oil refining industry, and the advancement of research into all substitutes in these oil-consuming countries in recent years. Thirdly, due to the general and extreme restrictions on imports and preparations for war in various countries around the world recently, the phenomenon of so-called "oil self-sufficiency" has shown a widespread development. As a result of these reasons, a contradictory phenomenon has emerged where oil production has increased but its market has shrunk, thus bringing about the scourge of the collapse of the world's oil market; and this scourge will not be alleviated by a slight increase in the objective need for oil.

Due to the collapse of the global oil market, it is natural that the strange phenomenon of overproduction of oil in the world will immediately arise. According to this year's statistics, the production and demand for oil worldwide in recent years show an extremely unbalanced situation of oversupply as follows:

The above table shows that both the production and demand for oil worldwide have increased significantly in recent years, but compared to each other, production exceeds demand, showing a clear phenomenon of overproduction.

The United States is the most developed place in the world's oil industry, but the situation of oil production exceeding demand in the United States is particularly serious. Last year, although there were restrictions under the Petroleum Industry Law in the United States, its oil production continued to increase. If the figures for the previous year and last year are combined, then the oil production in the United States exceeded demand by 18.5 million tons.

In addition to the United States, oil production in the world's major producing countries has also continued to increase in the past two years. Please see the following table (unit: million tons):

What is shown here can also prove that oil production in the world's major oil-producing countries is increasing rapidly recently. Such a large increase in production is certainly not something that a slight increase in demand can accommodate. Therefore, in recent years, with the exception of the Soviet Union, which has a special situation, almost all of the world's major oil-producing countries, led by the United States, have fallen into a crisis of oil overproduction.

Because of the collapse of the global oil market and the overproduction of oil in the world, the market prices of oil industry stocks on major stock exchanges around the world have fallen far below those before the panic (before 1929) in recent years. This can be seen from the following table of stock price indices of the oil industry on exchanges around the world: (1929 equals 100)

Last year, the stock prices of oil companies on exchanges everywhere were lower than those of the previous year. This fact fully demonstrates the pessimism in the world's oil industry and oil market.

However, the struggle among the world's trusts for oil resources and sales markets is only increasing. Under these circumstances, if the global oil market wants to improve, it is feared that it will only have to wait for the outbreak of a widespread global war, because at that time, the demand for oil will greatly increase, and the surplus oil production can be consumed in the war. Therefore, some people say that figures such as kerosene magnates are like military industrialists, and they very much hope that a brutal war will break out as soon as possible - this seems to have some reason.

Art World

On the Performance Method of Storytelling Drama 240

— Lichen

Drama, I am completely an outsider to this field. Especially to the old Chinese opera, not only can I not hum a single line, but I also watch it very rarely. Recently, at the invitation of a friend, I occasionally went to see an old opera, which also made me, an outsider, have some feelings about it, and I have some so-called opinions that I think it would be okay to bring up and talk about.

Drama, dance, and music are now all regarded as a kind of artistic entertainment, but these three have different characteristics. Because of this, in today's world where scientific classification has developed, they have all been divided into specialized subjects in art. In terms of their respective characteristics, drama is a more realistic art, because it concretely performs the words and actions of characters in a story, and even imitates the activities of characters in a story. Dance is different. It is much more abstract than drama. It uses a kind of physical movement to comprehensively express the overall appearance of a certain situation. Therefore, it does not have to focus on the detailed description of the activities and behaviors of characters in the process, but rather shortens and abstracts it into a symbolic concept that can be understood, and the performers express it through physical movements, and even directly express the performers' imagination or their own emotions. Therefore, although dance, like drama, uses physical movements to perform, drama expresses realistic facts and behavioral processes, while dance only expresses a conceptualized scene. For example, many dances of savage peoples, such as the war dances of the Negro and Indian tribes, simplify the facts of war and shorten them into a performance of a conceptualized scene. In the wedding dances and harvest dances of savage peoples, they imaginatively express the happiness of love, but do not necessarily perform a fixed real event and courtship actions, etc. The same is true of harvest dances, which only express the feeling of joy for a bountiful harvest, etc. As for music, it goes without saying. It is the expression of people's inner feelings and desires. Although it can sometimes embody a lively scene of a situation, such as when we hear the sound of a boatman's song, we seem to be able to vaguely think of the actions of those boatmen pulling the boat, thinking of them carrying heavy boat ropes, bending over, and moving forward step by step with great difficulty, and even thinking of the various real scenes of them coming from far away and then going from near to far, until they cannot be seen, as if we were seeing it with our own eyes. But in any case, the realistic scenes expressed by music are embodied by the revelation of inner feelings to the external situation, while dance and drama embody inner feelings through external actions. Because of this, the characteristics of these three things are different, and modern genuine art, therefore, makes them independent, developing them according to their respective characteristics, so that they can become more scientific and more artistic arts.

Chinese old opera is clearly a combination of these three things. It has movements and declarative performances, which means that its performance adopts a realistic descriptive method. It realistically performs the actions and words of the characters in the story, imitates the behavior and language of the characters in the story, and even concretely and in detail describes its facts, which includes the components of pure dramatic essence. However, when describing the behavior of characters in a story with physical movements, it is not limited to the realistic activities of the characters, but mixes it with the performance of abstract and intentional movements. Therefore, the audience also has to understand the characters' personality, thoughts, etc. from the form of physical performance. This means that Chinese old opera expresses the characters' personality, thoughts, behavior, etc. in the story with conceptualized scenes, rather than performing the realistic actions of the characters in the story. Therefore, this includes the performance method of dance essence. This is also the case in reality. Whether it is sheng, dan, chou, or mo, their activities on the stage are mostly done in the form of dancing. For example, when a wusheng or a black-faced character comes on stage, there is always a lot of jumping and dancing, which is used to express their strength and power, and their strong and mighty nature. Even in their actions, their steps and walking postures have a dancing color, because in fact, ordinary people never dance randomly or walk in that way. As for Chinese old opera, its language is mainly based on songs, and dialogues account for very little in the whole play, which is not a regular dramatic performance method. In terms of language, it is not realistic in describing things, because in real life, where is there the matter of singing words as songs? The lyrics, songs, and tones sung by the performers in old opera do not focus on using language to describe the real words of the characters in the play, but on using the tones of music to embody the full shape of the characters' personalities and their inner emotions. For example, the tone of Qingyi is deliberately made particularly gentle, humble, and timid. This not only shows the weakness and tenderness of women from her voice, but also fully shows how women under the rule of feudal society are oppressed into gentle and docile weaklings, becoming men's playthings and tame sheep.

From all these perspectives, Chinese old opera has too many symbolic elements, so everyone says it is symbolist. In fact, this kind of drama cannot be simply called drama, but is a mixture of drama, dance, and music. This kind of drama, if it is for the purpose of making drama, dance, and even music specialized and scientific, is not very suitable. Because drama focuses on realism, then changing the realistic behavior and actions into the way of dancing, and changing the declaration of language into the way of music, makes it not easy to be realistic and make drama progress. For example, if this play wants to perform an assassin assassinating, it should be done with witty and agile actions in order to show the realistic situation of urgency, wit, and panic, and it can also be vivid and touching. But the old opera comes up with a set of dancing and random dancing, and the content of tension, wit, and agility is completely obscured. How can this make that scene colorful? Also, in the performance of dialogues, some originally contain profound principles, or vicious and deep conversations, which must be expressed in language. Now you change it into singing to each other, and it is very difficult to express the real situation of deep, tight, vicious dialogues or debates. From the experience of the use of Chinese vernacular in recent years, it has been proven that even using classical Chinese is not easy to express some philosophical and scientific sentences, let alone wanting to use singing-style sentences to express the dialogues of the characters in the play. As for the timely relaxation, high and low intonation, etc. in the conversation, it is even more difficult to express in songs. Therefore, the use of songs in Chinese opera in the expression of statements only has a part of the meaning of musical beauty, and cannot realistically express the real situation of the characters' words and the wonderful plot, which also makes it difficult for it to complete its dramatic task and achieve scientificization.

Of course, I am not saying that drama cannot be mixed with dance and music at all. I think that the difficulty of drama with dance and music also lies in inserting it into the realism of drama. That is to say, use it only when there is dancing and singing in the dramatic story. If there is not, then all performances should realistically perform the possible actions and language of the characters in the story, so that the drama can be scientific and become a specialized and pure drama.

Chinese old opera also has a major shortcoming, which is the issue of musical instruments. This is not only too noisy, but also not realistic, and can even disrupt people from concentrating on understanding the plot. The musical value of these kinds of musical instruments is originally very low. The reason why Chinese opera cannot abolish it is probably related to its mixed use of dance performance methods. Because it has to use the rhythm of drums and gongs to regulate and restrain the postures and techniques of dance, and even the syllables of singing, etc. The so-called "catching gongs" is usually the reason for this. Therefore, to abolish musical instruments, I am afraid that it is necessary to start with changing the performance method of dancing.

Chinese old opera is very primitive. When it comes to its content, it is of course entirely a product of feudal consciousness. As for the background of the production of this kind of drama, and how much use its symbolic characteristics of performance methods have, etc., are also worthy of discussion, but there is not much space to discuss this, so I will leave it to talk about it when there is a chance in the future.

Commentary

On National Salvation 241

— Zhu Junshi

The internal affairs and diplomacy of any country are entrusted to its government. A government has its own certain policies. The people authorize the government, and the government should exert its abilities to strive for independence and survival for the nation and the country. If it does not betray the heavy trust of the people, the people must not go back and hinder the government's policy implementation steps.

But unfortunately, China, beset by internal and external troubles, is being forced to the brink. The national situation is precarious to the extreme. Recently, due to the autonomy movement in North China, there is a dangerous sign of breaking away from the central government. The universities in Peiping first made the determination to give their "last lesson," and then carried out a vigorous patriotic movement. The young students shouted for justice and expressed the public opinion in one ten-thousandth of the population. Their actions are commendable, praiseworthy, and admirable, and are no less than the May Fourth Movement. However, in a country's politics, if the government cannot fully exert its abilities and needs young students to intervene, causing them to distract from their studies and waste their precious time, it is really an extremely unfortunate thing! And in China, this kind of unfortunate thing happens one after another, which is the greatest misfortune among misfortunes!

Following the large-scale demonstrations in the universities of Peiping and Tientsin, Shanghai, Wuhan, and other places have also reportedly followed suit. These passionate actions of strikes, parades, slogans, posters, etc., in extraordinary times, naturally have their own significant meaning in arousing a huge wave in the hearts of the majority of people. But it is pitiful that since the beginning of the Republic of China, there have been too many opportunities to adopt this kind of action, and after too many opportunities, it is still the same old strikes, parades, slogans, and posters. I wonder when and on what day our dying China will be able to make these unarmed masses forever abandon this kind of action and not use it?

Suppose that the first time we decided to shout slogans was after the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, then sixty years have passed, and we have been preparing and strengthening ourselves until now. What is still impossible to do? And suppose that the next time we decided to shout slogans was twenty years ago during the period when Yuan Shikai usurped national power, then ten years of education and ten years of recuperation should have made anything possible. And suppose that after the Northern Expedition, we really all shouted slogans of awakening, then seven or eight years of long years, why is national defense in a state of disarray and not even one hundredth of the things undone? Afterwards, the Jinan Incident, the loss of the Northeast, and the fall of Rehe Province, the times gave us deep and huge painful bites, but what could be summoned to national affairs besides the young students' patriotic enthusiasm? Thinking of this, I can't help but tear my heart and bleed, and I don't know where the tears should come from!

When we examine the past, we should have a deeper understanding of the national salvation movement. As mentioned above, demonstrations and parades are sufficient to show where the true public opinion of our country lies under extraordinary circumstances, sufficient to correct the vision and hearing of the world, and chill the hearts of traitors. Their intentions are good, but at the same time, we should also pay attention to how to strengthen the strength of national salvation to arm our bodies and arm our spirits:

1. National salvation should be listed as a constant belief. The overall plan for national salvation must be handled calmly, and it can never be achieved with the efforts of one morning or evening. In the past, King Goujian of Yue relied on his constant belief in lying on firewood and tasting gall, and finally achieved the goal of defeating Wu. If we want to talk about saving the country today, we must save the country every day, every moment, and every second; studying is for saving the country, working is for saving the country, speaking is for saving the country, saving the country at all times, saving the country in all things, and saving the country is our only belief. Only in this way can we gather absolutely great strength and truly show the practical effectiveness of saving the country.

2. National salvation should strengthen the overall strength of the country. The coming war is a scientific war, a war of knowledge, and a war in which the entire nation fights against the enemy. Today, our country's science is not as good as others, the people's knowledge is not as good as others, and the overall national strength is not as good as others. Therefore, from now on, we should engage in strengthening the country's strength on the one hand, and hold the determination to wait for the dawn, preparing to go to the national crisis together.

3. Young students should arm their minds as soon as possible.

The rise of national salvation movements in various places recently has made China and foreign countries know that our people's hearts have not died, and that the torch of national liberation is about to become a prairie fire. But because of this, there will inevitably be a small number of young students who are future national talents who will be sacrificed in vain under iron bars and stab wounds. On the one hand, it makes us admire their spirit of sacrifice, but on the other hand, when we think of the sentence "He died before he could finish his task," we can't help but feel infinite sorrow! Therefore, I think that in addition to demonstrations and parades, we should turn to the masses to awaken them from their sleeping nightmares. We should arm our own brains, be calm, work hard, until the nation is liberated!

Talking about the issue of national salvation has long been heartbreaking, and it is even more difficult for the Chinese people in the current situation to talk about the issue of national salvation. In the above respects, I am willing to seek the common understanding of the people of the country with the greatest sincerity!

Amateur Coffee Shop

Talking About "Worldliness" 242

— Weiren

I remember when I was young, I used to quarrel with my little companions for some reason, felt wronged, and even started fighting, scratching bloody marks on my face and swelling up a big blue mark on my leg. From then on, I broke off contact with my little companions and did not interact with them.

Years later, recalling the situation when I was young, I often find myself laughing.

Now, I have been in this society for five or six years, and I know that my temperament is very different from before. My previous stubbornness, arrogance, aloofness, and arrogant attitude have been melted away a lot by the great furnace of society. This may be a good thing, because now when I occasionally return to my hometown, the older elders will unanimously praise me and say: "This child knows the times!"

Worldliness is the key to living in the world. As the saying goes: "If you don't know how to read, you can still eat; if you don't know the sky and don't know people, it will be difficult to eat!" Indeed, indeed.

Generally, to know people, you must "observe their expressions"; to know the sky, you must "be good at discerning cold and warmth."

Therefore, a worldly woman, if she has flesh to sell, must sell flesh; a worldly man may as well sell his soul. To put it plainly, as long as there is wealth and glory, it is not impossible to be a running dog. They will always think this way: What is the purpose of life? Whoever doesn't become a slave is just a "bumpkin" as Shanghainese say. As long as gold, silver, and jewelry are in hand, a new Ford car from 1936 can be ridden, a marble-built foreign house can be lived in, and new French cuisine on the Atlantic coast can be enjoyed. It doesn't matter if you are a concubine or a plaything!

In short, whoever doesn't understand that this is the sharp new era of the 20th century and stubbornly clings to loyalty, chastity, integrity, and righteousness is a living zombie that is too pedantic and too corrupt!

Or, whoever harbors hatred for the fat businessman who ruined your chastity, or who scolds the master who deprived you of your freedom, and is preoccupied with revenge, is even more ignorant of "worldliness."

Today's smartest people want: yesterday's "enemy" can become "friend" today. Yesterday he was the one who cut your flesh, today you may as well carry thorns and ask him for forgiveness, and even if he slapped your right cheek, you may as well give him your left cheek. When we see them "raising champagne," they drink it all in one gulp, and then they are as friendly as ever and smile at each other. Isn't there a sense of "humor" here?

Some people who don't see through the true meaning of worldliness often think that worldly affairs are too childish and human affairs are too ridiculous when they see similar things. But what else is there in worldly affairs besides childishness? What else is there in human affairs besides ridiculousness? Two gentlemen meet on the street, shake hands with each other, "The weather today hahaha," aren't these ridiculous, aren't these childish? Therefore, the superior person: "How can a person not know worldliness?"

Recently, my compassionate and humanitarian thoughts often inspire my grand ambition to save the world; I want to go and save those sentient beings who are busy and ignorant of worldliness. Because I deeply believe in the truth of "Those who obey Heaven prosper, and those who defy Heaven perish." If a good head is not used to obey Heaven, then why bother to be a head?

Alas! The so-called worldliness and human relations in the world have not yet been believed by the vast number of sentient beings, which is also very sad.

Extracting Account Books (9) 243

— Pu Yu

"Hey! Don't dawdle. It's not like I want your money. Think about it yourself: the case is so serious!"

"Director Liu, I am an innocent person! Please have mercy; today I'll scrape together twenty yuan for travel expenses, and then give you a grace period of five days to send a hundred yuan to the bureau. -- I'll have to borrow! But..."

Damn! After a day of effort, getting "twenty yuan" is a joke, isn't it? What use is a hundred yuan of debt? It would be different if it were a large sum.

"Boss Li. I don't like to make empty promises; if you are willing to settle this case, quickly come up with two hundred yuan in cash now, and the remaining two hundred can be delayed for three days, but you have to issue a promissory note."

"Even if you kill me, I can't come up with that amount!"

"Then what are you going to do? -- Not a single yuan can be less!" I felt that I couldn't back down any further, this momentum must be firm.

"Me?..." The old man sighed deeply, and sat sadly on the edge of the bed.

There was a moment of silence.

Outside it was already dusk, and a kerosene lamp had been lit in the room. At this time, I was both angry and flustered: not a single penny had been received, and the old man's firm stubbornness really left me helpless. So I decided to take a tough approach and give him one last squeeze.

"Okay!" I ordered Jiang Xiwu pointedly, "Get the sealing strips out, let's do this officially!" As soon as I finished speaking, I stepped to the account table, pretending to take the account book. (To be continued)

Broadcasting Schedule

Special Program 244

Movie News

Electrosound New Year Special Issue Published 245

Su Zhen's Electrosound Movie Pictorial Weekly, with its exquisite pictures and rich content, has been popular at home and abroad since its publication and is loved by everyone. As the year 25th anniversary of the Republic of China is approaching, the publication is issuing a New Year's special issue to celebrate and thank its readers. The length of the issue is doubled compared to usual, with eight pages of copper-plate illustrations, a feast for the eyes. The front and back covers feature three-color photo reproductions of Mei Lin and Dolores del Río, which are particularly beautiful and lovely. The text includes many articles that are impossible to find elsewhere, such as "Hu Die Opens a Film Company and Suffers a Blow," "The Inside Story of Xu Lai's Check Dispute," "Hu Ping Secretly Returns to Shanghai from Qingdao," "Now is the Time for Wang Ying to Cry," "Yuan Meiyun and Wang Yin Cohabitate," "The Wildcat King's First Love," "Realistic Portraits of Film People's Lives," "A Glimpse of Chengdu's Film Industry in the 24th Year," "Review of Important Productions from American Film Companies," "Luo Lie Taiyang Temporarily Leaves the Film World," "Predictions for the Film Industry in 1936," and "Xie Xiasun's Chess Tournament After Arriving in Hong Kong." Each copy costs one dime, and is available at all bookstores and newsstands. Mail orders with a one-dime postage fee can be sent to Sanhe Publishing, 138 Nanjing Road, Shanghai, and they will be shipped immediately.

A "Soft and Hard" Shot in "Little Tyrant" - Special New Year's Eve Screening at the Great Light Theater

Silver Scribbles 246

— Zhi Er

There is a very good cover on this issue of "Public Life": a bare-handed student is being beaten by two soldiers, and a smiling foreigner is standing beside them. What a heartbreaking and tragic event!

However, where are our newsreel cameras?

Let's not talk about Gongping, it's too far away; Shanghai, isn't there also a booming student movement for national salvation? However, where are our cameras?

Or, we can say that filming newsreels is the idea of the bosses. But! What kind of expressions do our employees have? Not even a single declaration!

If there was a newsreel about this student movement for national salvation being shown publicly in Shanghai, I don't believe it wouldn't sell out for three days!

However, there is not a single company in all of China that films newsreels, or if there is, it's just some "official" news.

Without talking about justice or heroism, let's just talk about it from a "business perspective," isn't this a pretty good subject?

Unless, our film industry is truly impoverished and out of its mind.

If that's really the case, then being poor is their own fault!
